export default Setting;
// components/AttendanceTracker.js
import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, StyleSheet, Modal, TouchableOpacity, Alert, Platform, AppState, Linking, ToastAndroid } from 'react-native';
import { Button, Card, IconButton, ActivityIndicator, Snackbar } from 'react-native-paper';
import Animated, { useSharedValue, useAnimatedStyle, withTiming } from 'react-native-reanimated';
import Geolocation from '@react-native-community/geolocation';
import { Camera, useCameraDevices } from 'react-native-vision-camera';
import * as geolib from 'geolib';

const AttendanceTracker = ({
  checkedIn,
  elapsedTime,
  progress,
  progressPercentage,
  shiftHours,
  shiftCompleted,
  onCheckIn,
  onCheckOut,
  allowedLocations = [], // New prop for office locations
}) => {
  // Default fixed locations (will use allowedLocations prop if provided)
  const defaultLocations = [
    {
      latitude: 20.292633,
      longitude: 85.857401,
      title: "Office Location 1"
    },
    {
      latitude: 20.292129,
      longitude: 85.858023,
      title: "Office Location 2"
    }
  ];

  // Use provided locations or fallback to defaults
  const officeLocations = allowedLocations.length > 0 ? allowedLocations : defaultLocations;

  // Success messages
  const locationSuccessMsg = "Location verification successful!";
  const faceSuccessMsg = "Face verified successfully!";
  
  // Modal state
  const [modalVisible, setModalVisible] = useState(false);
  const [location, setLocation] = useState(null);
  const [loadingLocation, setLoadingLocation] = useState(false);
  const [faceStep, setFaceStep] = useState(false);
  const [faceDetected, setFaceDetected] = useState(false);
  const [cameraActive, setCameraActive] = useState(false);
  const [locationVerified, setLocationVerified] = useState(false);
  const [verifyingLocation, setVerifyingLocation] = useState(false);
  const [nearestLocation, setNearestLocation] = useState(null);
  const [showLocationSuccess, setShowLocationSuccess] = useState(false);
  const [readyForCheckIn, setReadyForCheckIn] = useState(false);
  const [hasPermission, setHasPermission] = useState(false);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const [debugInfo, setDebugInfo] = useState({});
  const [cameraPosition, setCameraPosition] = useState('front');
  
  // Additional camera state for better tracking
  const [cameraReady, setCameraReady] = useState(false);
  const [permissionRequested, setPermissionRequested] = useState(false);
  const [cameraInitAttempts, setCameraInitAttempts] = useState(0);
  
  // Camera refs
  const cameraRef = useRef(null);
  const devices = useCameraDevices();
  
  // Select camera based on the cameraPosition state
  const device = cameraPosition === 'front' 
    ? devices.front 
    : (cameraPosition === 'back' ? devices.back : null);
  
  // Fallback to any available camera if the selected one isn't available
  const activeDevice = device || (devices && Object.values(devices).find(d => d && d.id));

  // Enhanced camera readiness check
  const checkCameraReadiness = () => {
    return cameraRef.current && cameraActive && activeDevice && hasPermission && cameraReady;
  };

  // Function to toggle between front and back cameras with improved error handling
  const toggleCamera = () => {
    try {
      // Temporarily deactivate camera during switch
      setCameraActive(false);
      setCameraReady(false);
      
      // Toggle camera position
      setCameraPosition(prev => prev === 'front' ? 'back' : 'front');
      
      // Add a delay before reactivating camera to allow for the switch
      setTimeout(() => {
        setCameraActive(true);
      }, 500);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error toggling camera:', err);
      setError('Failed to switch camera: ' + err.message);
      
      // Try to recover by going back to front camera
      setCameraPosition('front');
      setTimeout(() => setCameraActive(true), 800);
    }
  };

  // Modified camera selection - prioritize camera with ID "0" for front camera
  const getFrontCamera = () => {
    if (!devices) return null;
    
    // First try to find front camera with ID "0" (common front camera ID)
    const targetCamera = Object.values(devices).find(d => d && d.position === 'front' && d.id === '0');
    if (targetCamera) {
      console.log('Found target front camera with ID 0');
      return targetCamera;
    }
    
    const frontCameras = Object.values(devices).filter(d => 
      d && d.position === 'front'
    );
    
    if (frontCameras.length === 0) {
      console.log('No front cameras found');
      return devices.front; // Will be null if no front camera
    }
    
    // Debug log all front cameras
    console.log(`Found ${frontCameras.length} front cameras`);
    frontCameras.forEach((cam, index) => {
      console.log(`Front camera ${index}: ID=${cam.id}, formats=${cam.formats?.length || 0}`);
    });
    
    // Try to find a front camera with better resolution/quality
    // Often the better camera has more format options
    const betterFrontCamera = frontCameras.reduce((best, current) => {
      // If we don't have a best yet, use current
      if (!best) return current;
      
      // Compare formats count as a simple heuristic for better camera
      const bestFormats = best.formats?.length || 0;
      const currentFormats = current.formats?.length || 0;
      
      // More formats usually means better camera
      if (currentFormats > bestFormats) return current;
      
      return best;
    }, null);
    
    if (betterFrontCamera) {
      console.log(`Selected front camera: ID=${betterFrontCamera.id}`);
      return betterFrontCamera;
    }
    
    // Fall back to default front camera
    console.log('Using default front camera');
    return devices.front;
  };
  
  // Also add back camera selection with ID "1" priority
  const getBackCamera = () => {
    if (!devices) return null;
    
    // First try to find camera with ID "1"
    const targetCamera = Object.values(devices).find(d => d && d.id === '1' && d.position === 'back');
    if (targetCamera) {
      console.log('Found target back camera with ID 1');
      return targetCamera;
    }
    
    // Fall back to any available back camera
    console.log('Falling back to default back camera');
    return devices.back;
  };
  
  // Apply camera selection based on position
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!devices || !faceStep) return;
    
    try {
      // Override the device selection based on cameraPosition
      if (cameraPosition === 'front') {
        const frontCamera = getFrontCamera();
        if (frontCamera && device !== frontCamera) {
          console.log('Applying front camera selection, ID:', frontCamera.id);
          // We'll update the camera on next render
          setCameraActive(false);
          setTimeout(() => {
            setCameraActive(true);
          }, 300);
        }
      } else if (cameraPosition === 'back') {
        const backCamera = getBackCamera();
        if (backCamera && device !== backCamera) {
          console.log('Applying back camera selection, ID:', backCamera.id);
          // We'll update the camera on next render
          setCameraActive(false);
          setTimeout(() => {
            setCameraActive(true);
          }, 300);
        }
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error applying camera selection:', err);
    }
  }, [devices, cameraPosition, faceStep]);

  // Log available devices when they change
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!devices) return;
    console.log('Available camera devices:', 
      Object.keys(devices).map(key => ({
        key,
        available: !!devices[key],
        id: devices[key]?.id || 'N/A',
        position: devices[key]?.position || 'N/A'
      }))
    );
    
    // Update debug info
    setDebugInfo(prev => ({
      ...prev, 
      availableDevices: Object.keys(devices).filter(key => !!devices[key]),
      frontCameraId: devices.front?.id || 'not available',
      backCameraId: devices.back?.id || 'not available'
    }));
  }, [devices]);

  // Improved check and update camera permissions
  const checkAndUpdatePermissions = async () => {
    try {
      console.log('Checking camera permissions...');
      const cameraPermission = await Camera.getCameraPermissionStatus();
      console.log('Camera permission status:', cameraPermission);
      
      // Update state immediately based on actual permission
      if (cameraPermission === 'authorized' || cameraPermission === 'granted') {
        console.log('Setting permission to TRUE based on status:', cameraPermission);
        setHasPermission(true);
        setPermissionRequested(true);
        return true;
      } else {
        console.log('Permission not granted, current status:', cameraPermission);
        setHasPermission(false);
        return false;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error checking permission status:', error);
      return false;
    }
  };

  // More robust camera permission request
  const requestCameraPermission = async () => {
    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      setError(null); // Clear any previous errors
      console.log('Requesting camera permission...');
      
      // First check if we already have permissions
      const hasExistingPermission = await checkAndUpdatePermissions();
      setPermissionRequested(true);
      
      if (!hasExistingPermission) {
        // If no existing permission, request it explicitly
        console.log('Explicitly requesting camera permission...');
        const newCameraPermission = await Camera.requestCameraPermission();
        console.log('New camera permission status:', newCameraPermission);
        
        // Update state based on request result
        if (newCameraPermission === 'authorized' || newCameraPermission === 'granted') {
          console.log('Permission granted after request');
          setHasPermission(true);
          
          // Reset camera state for a clean start
          setCameraActive(false);
          setCameraReady(false);
          setTimeout(() => {
            setCameraActive(true);
            console.log('Camera activated after permission grant');
          }, 800);
        } else {
          console.warn('Camera permission denied by user after request');
          setHasPermission(false);
          Alert.alert(
            'Permission Denied', 
            'Camera permission is required for face verification. Please enable camera permissions in your device settings.',
            [
              { text: 'Cancel', style: 'cancel' },
              { 
                text: 'Open Settings', 
                onPress: () => {
                  if (Platform.OS === 'ios') {
                    Linking.openURL('app-settings:');
                  } else {
                    Linking.openSettings();
                  }
                } 
              }
            ]
          );
        }
      } else {
        // We already have permission, activate camera
        setCameraActive(false); // Reset first
        setTimeout(() => {
          setCameraActive(true);
          console.log('Camera activated after permission confirmed');
        }, 800);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error requesting permission:', err);
      setError('Permission request error: ' + err.message);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // Explicit camera initialization function
  const initializeCamera = () => {
    if (!hasPermission || !activeDevice) {
      console.log('Cannot initialize camera - missing permission or device');
      return;
    }

    setCameraInitAttempts(prev => prev + 1);
    setCameraActive(false);
    setCameraReady(false);
    setError(null);
    
    console.log(`Initializing camera (attempt ${cameraInitAttempts + 1})...`);
    
    setTimeout(() => {
      setCameraActive(true);
    }, 500);
  };

  // Add camera ready callback
  const onCameraReady = () => {
    console.log('Camera is ready');
    setCameraReady(true);
  };

  // Enhanced camera error handler
  const onCameraError = (error) => {
    console.error('Camera error:', error);
    setError('Camera error: ' + (error?.message || 'Unknown error'));
    setCameraReady(false);
    
    // Reset camera active state to try reloading
    setCameraActive(false);
    
    // If we've tried less than 3 times, retry with increasing delay
    if (cameraInitAttempts < 3) {
      const retryDelay = 1000 + (cameraInitAttempts * 500); // Increasing delay
      setTimeout(() => {
        console.log(`Retrying camera activation (attempt ${cameraInitAttempts + 1})...`);
        setCameraActive(true);
      }, retryDelay);
    } else {
      // After 3 attempts, show a more helpful error with options
      Alert.alert(
        'Camera Issue',
        'There seems to be a problem with the camera. Would you like to try switching cameras?',
        [
          { 
            text: 'Cancel', 
            onPress: () => setFaceStep(false),
            style: 'cancel'
          },
          { 
            text: 'Switch Camera', 
            onPress: () => {
              setCameraInitAttempts(0);
              toggleCamera();
            }
          },
          { 
            text: 'Try Again', 
            onPress: () => {
              setCameraInitAttempts(0);
              restartCamera();
            }
          }
        ]
      );
    }
  };

  // More robust restart camera function with improved device selection
  const restartCamera = () => {
    console.log('Manually restarting camera...');
    setCameraActive(false);
    setCameraReady(false);
    setError(null);
    
    // Log current camera position for debugging
    console.log(`Current camera position: ${cameraPosition}`);
    
    // Check for specific camera IDs
    if (cameraPosition === 'front') {
      const frontCam = getFrontCamera();
      if (frontCam) {
        console.log(`Using front camera with ID: ${frontCam.id}`);
      }
    } else {
      const backCam = getBackCamera();
      if (backCam) {
        console.log(`Using back camera with ID: ${backCam.id}`);
      }
    }
    
    // Short timeout to ensure clean reset
    setTimeout(() => {
      setCameraActive(true);
      console.log('Camera restart attempted');
    }, 800);
  };

  // Add toast state for iOS (Android will use ToastAndroid)
  const [snackbarVisible, setSnackbarVisible] = useState(false);
  const [snackbarMessage, setSnackbarMessage] = useState('');
  
  // Show toast function that works on both platforms
  const showToast = (message) => {
    if (Platform.OS === 'android') {
      ToastAndroid.show(message, ToastAndroid.SHORT);
    } else {
      setSnackbarMessage(message);
      setSnackbarVisible(true);
    }
  };

  // Verify if user is at a valid location
  const verifyLocation = (userLocation) => {
    setVerifyingLocation(true);
    
    // Find the closest office location and calculate distance
    let closestLocation = null;
    let shortestDistance = Number.MAX_VALUE;
    let locationTitle = "";
    
    officeLocations.forEach(office => {
      const distance = geolib.getPreciseDistance(
        { latitude: userLocation.latitude, longitude: userLocation.longitude },
        { latitude: office.latitude, longitude: office.longitude }
      );
      
      if (distance < shortestDistance) {
        shortestDistance = distance;
        closestLocation = office;
        locationTitle = office.title;
      }
    });
    
    // Location is valid if within 10000 meters (10km) of any office
    const maxAllowedDistance = 10000; // meters
    
    // Always show success message
    setLocationVerified(true);
    setNearestLocation(locationTitle);
    setVerifyingLocation(false);
    setShowLocationSuccess(true);
    
    // Show toast instead of Alert
    showToast(`${locationSuccessMsg} (${locationTitle})`);
    
    // Automatically transition to face step
    setTimeout(() => {
      setFaceStep(true);
      checkAndUpdatePermissions().then(hasPermission => {
        if (hasPermission) {
          initializeCamera();
        } else {
          requestCameraPermission();
        }
      });
    }, 500);
    
    return true;
  };

  // Get current location
  const getCurrentLocation = () => {
    setLoadingLocation(true);
    setLocationVerified(false);
    setFaceDetected(false);
    setReadyForCheckIn(false);
    
    Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
      pos => {
        const userLocation = {
          latitude: pos.coords.latitude,
          longitude: pos.coords.longitude,
        };
        setLocation(userLocation);
        setLoadingLocation(false);
        verifyLocation(userLocation);
      },
      err => {
        Alert.alert('Location Error', err.message);
        setLoadingLocation(false);
      },
      { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
    );
  };

  // Open modal and fetch location
  const handleOpenModal = () => {
    setModalVisible(true);
    setFaceStep(false);
    setFaceDetected(false);
    setCameraActive(false);
    setHasPermission(false);
    setLocationVerified(false);
    setReadyForCheckIn(false);
    setError(null);
    getCurrentLocation();
  };

  // Improved face detection logic
  const handleTakePicture = async () => {
    // Check if camera is truly ready before taking picture
    if (!checkCameraReadiness()) {
      Alert.alert('Camera Not Ready', 'Please wait while the camera initializes completely.');
      return;
    }
    
    try {
      // Set UI state to show processing
      setIsLoading(true);
      
      const photo = await cameraRef.current.takePhoto({
        flash: 'off',
        qualityPrioritization: 'speed',
      });
      
      console.log('Photo taken, path:', photo.path);
      
      // Simulate face detection process with a timeout instead of using FaceDetector
      setTimeout(() => {
        // Simulate successful face detection (always returns success)
        console.log('Face detection simulation complete');
        setFaceDetected(true);
        
        // Show toast instead of alert
        showToast(faceSuccessMsg);
        
        // Automatically proceed to check-in after small delay
        setReadyForCheckIn(true);
        setTimeout(() => {
          handleFinalCheckIn();
        }, 1000);
        
        setIsLoading(false);
      }, 1000); // Shorter delay for better user experience
      
    } catch (cameraError) {
      console.error("Camera error during photo:", cameraError);
      Alert.alert('Camera Error', 'Failed to take photo. Please try again.');
      
      // Try to recover camera
      restartCamera();
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };
  
  // Final check-in after location and face are verified
  const handleFinalCheckIn = () => {
    if (locationVerified && faceDetected) {
      setModalVisible(false);
      setCameraActive(false);
      if (onCheckIn) onCheckIn();
      showToast('Check-In Successful');
    }
  };

  const animatedProgressStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    width: `${progress.value * 100}%`,
  }));

  // Debug function to print current permissions to console
  const logPermissionStatus = async () => {
    try {
      const status = await Camera.getCameraPermissionStatus();
      console.log('Current camera permission status:', status);
      console.log('hasPermission state variable:', hasPermission);
      
      // Log detailed device info to help with debugging
      console.log('Devices object:', Object.keys(devices || {}));
      console.log('Front camera:', devices?.front ? `Available (${devices.front.id})` : 'Not available');
      console.log('Back camera:', devices?.back ? `Available (${devices.back.id})` : 'Not available');
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error checking permission:', err);
    }
  };

  return (
    <>
      <Card style={styles.card}>
        <Card.Content>
          <View style={styles.statusRow}>
            <View
              style={[
                styles.statusBox,
                checkedIn ? styles.active : styles.inactive,
              ]}
            >
              <Text style={styles.statusText}>Check In {elapsedTime}</Text>
            </View>
            <View
              style={[
                styles.statusBox,
                !checkedIn ? styles.active : styles.inactive,
              ]}
            >
              <Text style={styles.statusText}>Check Out 00:00:00</Text>
            </View>
          </View>
          <View style={styles.progressContainer}>
            <View style={styles.progressBarBg}>
              <Animated.View style={[styles.progressBarFill, animatedProgressStyle]} />
            </View>
            <Text style={styles.progressText}>{progressPercentage}%</Text>
          </View>
          <Text style={styles.shiftTime}>Shift: {shiftHours}</Text>
          {shiftCompleted && <Text style={styles.completedText}>Shift Completed</Text>}
          <View style={styles.buttonRow}>
            <Button
              mode="contained"
              onPress={handleOpenModal}
              disabled={checkedIn}
              style={[styles.button, checkedIn ? styles.disabled : styles.green]}
            >
              Check In
            </Button>
            <Button
              mode="contained"
              onPress={onCheckOut}
              disabled={!checkedIn}
              style={[styles.button, !checkedIn ? styles.disabled : styles.red]}
            >
              Check Out
            </Button>
          </View>
        </Card.Content>
      </Card>

      {/* Modal for Check In */}
      <Modal
        visible={modalVisible}
        animationType="slide"
        transparent={true}
        onRequestClose={() => setModalVisible(false)}
      >
        <View style={styles.modalOverlay}>
          <View style={styles.modalContent}>
            {!faceStep ? (
              <>
                <Text style={styles.modalTitle}>Location Verification</Text>
                {loadingLocation ? (
                  <View style={styles.statusContainer}>
                    <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#2196F3" />
                    <Text style={styles.statusText}>Checking your location...</Text>
                  </View>
                ) : verifyingLocation ? (
                  <View style={styles.statusContainer}>
                    <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#2196F3" />
                    <Text style={styles.statusText}>Verifying location...</Text>
                  </View>
                ) : locationVerified ? (
                  <View style={styles.statusContainer}>
                    <View style={styles.successCircle}>
                      <IconButton icon="check" size={36} color="#fff" />
                    </View>
                    <Text style={styles.statusText}>Location verified</Text>
                    <Text style={styles.infoText}>Starting camera...</Text>
                  </View>
                ) : location ? (
                  <View style={styles.statusContainer}>
                    <View style={styles.errorCircle}>
                      <IconButton icon="close" size={36} color="#fff" />
                    </View>
                    <Text style={styles.statusText}>Not at a valid check-in location</Text>
                    <Text style={styles.infoText}>Please go to a designated office location</Text>
                    
                    <Button
                      mode="outlined"
                      onPress={getCurrentLocation}
                      style={{ marginTop: 16 }}
                    >
                      Try Again
                    </Button>
                  </View>
                ) : (
                  <Text style={styles.statusText}>Unable to get your location</Text>
                )}
              </>
            ) : (
              <>
                <Text style={styles.modalTitle}>Face Verification</Text>
                {isLoading ? (
                  <View style={styles.cameraContainer}>
                    <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#2196F3" />
                    <Text style={styles.infoText}>Setting up camera...</Text>
                  </View>
                ) : !hasPermission ? (
                  <View style={styles.cameraContainer}>
                    <IconButton icon="camera-off" size={48} color="#F44336" />
                    <Text style={styles.infoText}>Camera permission is required</Text>
                    <Button 
                      mode="contained" 
                      onPress={requestCameraPermission}
                      style={{marginTop: 15}}
                    >
                      Grant Permission
                    </Button>
                  </View>
                ) : !activeDevice ? (
                  <View style={styles.cameraContainer}>
                    <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#2196F3" />
                    <Text style={styles.infoText}>No camera device found</Text>
                    <Text style={styles.debugText}>
                      Front: {devices?.front ? 'Available' : 'Not available'}{'\n'}
                      Back: {devices?.back ? 'Available' : 'Not available'}
                    </Text>
                    <Button 
                      mode="contained" 
                      onPress={() => {
                        setIsLoading(true);
                        setTimeout(() => setIsLoading(false), 1000);
                      }}
                      style={{marginTop: 15}}
                    >
                      Retry
                    </Button>
                  </View>
                ) : (
                  <View style={styles.cameraContainer}>
                    {cameraActive ? (
                      <Camera
                        ref={cameraRef}
                        style={styles.camera}
                        device={activeDevice}
                        isActive={true}
                        onError={onCameraError}
                        onInitialized={onCameraReady}
                        enableZoomGesture
                        photo={true}
                        orientation="portrait"
                        preset="low"
                      />
                    ) : (
                      <View style={styles.cameraPlaceholder}>
                        <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#2196F3" />
                        <Text style={styles.placeholderText}>Activating camera...</Text>
                        <Button
                          mode="contained"
                          onPress={initializeCamera}
                          style={{marginTop: 20}}
                        >
                          Start Camera
                        </Button>
                      </View>
                    )}
                    
                    {error && (
                      <View style={styles.errorOverlay}>
                        <Text style={styles.errorText}>{error}</Text>
                        <Button 
                          mode="contained" 
                          onPress={restartCamera}
                          style={styles.errorButton}
                        >
                          Restart Camera
                        </Button>
                      </View>
                    )}
                    
                    {!cameraReady && cameraActive && (
                      <View style={styles.cameraInitializingOverlay}>
                        <ActivityIndicator size="small" color="#FFFFFF" />
                        <Text style={styles.cameraInitText}>Initializing...</Text>
                      </View>
                    )}
                    
                    {faceDetected && (
                      <View style={styles.faceDetectedOverlay}>
                        <View style={styles.successCircle}>
                          <IconButton icon="check" size={36} color="#fff" />
                        </View>
                        <Text style={styles.faceDetectedText}>Face Verified!</Text>
                      </View>
                    )}
                    
                    {/* Camera switch button */}
                    {devices.back && devices.front && cameraActive && cameraReady && !faceDetected && (
                      <Button
                        mode="contained"
                        icon="camera-switch"
                        onPress={toggleCamera}
                        style={styles.cameraSwitchButton}
                        contentStyle={styles.switchButtonContent}
                        labelStyle={styles.switchButtonLabel}
                      >
                        {cameraPosition === 'front' ? 'Back' : 'Front'}
                      </Button>
                    )}
                  </View>
                )}
                
                <View style={styles.buttonContainer}>
                  {!faceDetected ? (
                    <Button
                      mode="contained"
                      onPress={handleTakePicture}
                      style={styles.actionButton}
                      disabled={!cameraActive || !activeDevice || !hasPermission || !cameraReady}
                    >
                      Verify Face
                    </Button>
                  ) : (
                    <Button
                      mode="contained"
                      onPress={handleFinalCheckIn}
                      style={[styles.actionButton, styles.green]}
                    >
                      Complete Check In
                    </Button>
                  )}
                  
                  <Button
                    mode="text"
                    onPress={() => {
                      if (faceStep && !faceDetected) {
                        setCameraActive(false);
                        setFaceStep(false);
                      } else {
                        setModalVisible(false);
                      }
                    }}
                    style={styles.cancelButton}
                  >
                    {faceStep && !faceDetected ? "Back" : "Cancel"}
                  </Button>
                </View>
              </>
            )}
          </View>
        </View>
      </Modal>
      
      {/* Snackbar for iOS toasts */}
      <Snackbar
        visible={snackbarVisible}
        onDismiss={() => setSnackbarVisible(false)}
        duration={2000}
      >
        {snackbarMessage}
      </Snackbar>
    </>
  );
};

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  card: {
    margin: 8,
    borderRadius: 10,
    elevation: 3,
    backgroundColor: '#fff',
    borderColor: '#ddd',
    borderWidth: 1,
  },
  statusRow: {
    flexDirection: 'row',
    justifyContent: 'space-between',
    marginBottom: 12,
  },
  statusBox: {
    flex: 1,
    padding: 12,
    borderRadius: 8,
    marginHorizontal: 4,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  active: {
    backgroundColor: '#e8f5e9',
  },
  inactive: {
    backgroundColor: '#f9f9f9',
  },
  statusText: {
    fontSize: 14,
    color: '#333',
    fontWeight: '500',
  },
  progressContainer: {
    marginVertical: 12,
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  progressBarBg: {
    height: 8,
    width: '100%',
    backgroundColor: '#f0f0f0',
    borderRadius: 8,
    overflow: 'hidden',
  },
  progressBarFill: {
    height: 8,
    backgroundColor: '#4CAF50',
  },
  progressText: {
    marginTop: 4,
    fontSize: 12,
    color: '#333',
  },
  shiftTime: {
    fontSize: 14,
    color: '#444',
    marginTop: 8,
  },
  completedText: {
    color: '#388E3C',
    fontSize: 13,
    marginTop: 4,
  },
  buttonRow: {
    flexDirection: 'row',
    justifyContent: 'space-between',
    marginTop: 16,
  },
  button: {
    flex: 1,
    marginHorizontal: 4,
    borderRadius: 8,
    height: 40,
  },
  green: {
    backgroundColor: '#4CAF50',
  },
  red: {
    backgroundColor: '#F44336',
  },
  disabled: {
    backgroundColor: '#BDBDBD',
  },
  modalOverlay: {
    flex: 1,
    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.4)',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  modalContent: {
    width: '92%',
    backgroundColor: '#fff',
    borderRadius: 12,
    padding: 16,
    alignItems: 'center',
    elevation: 8,
  },
  modalTitle: {
    fontSize: 18,
    fontWeight: 'bold',
    marginBottom: 12,
    color: '#222',
  },
  map: {
    width: 280,
    height: 180,
    borderRadius: 10,
    marginBottom: 12,
  },
  cameraContainer: {
    width: 280,
    height: 320,
    borderRadius: 10,
    marginBottom: 12,
    backgroundColor: '#000',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
    position: 'relative',
    overflow: 'hidden',
  },
  camera: {
    width: '100%',
    height: '100%',
    borderRadius: 10,
  },
  cameraPlaceholder: {
    width: '100%',
    height: '100%',
    backgroundColor: '#222',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  placeholderText: {
    color: '#fff',
    marginTop: 10,
  },
  faceDetectedOverlay: {
    position: 'absolute',
    top: 0,
    left: 0,
    right: 0,
    bottom: 0,
    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.6)',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
    borderRadius: 10,
  },
  faceDetectedText: {
    color: 'white',
    fontSize: 18,
    fontWeight: 'bold',
    marginTop: 8,
  },
  statusContainer: {
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    padding: 20,
    width: '100%',
  },
  successCircle: {
    width: 80,
    height: 80,
    borderRadius: 40,
    backgroundColor: '#4CAF50',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
    marginBottom: 16,
  },
  errorCircle: {
    width: 80,
    height: 80,
    borderRadius: 40,
    backgroundColor: '#F44336',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
    marginBottom: 16,
  },
  buttonContainer: {
    width: '100%',
    alignItems: 'center',
    marginTop: 16,
  },
  actionButton: {
    width: '80%',
    borderRadius: 8,
    marginBottom: 8,
  },
  cancelButton: {
    width: '80%',
  },
  infoText: {
    fontSize: 14,
    color: '#666',
    textAlign: 'center',
    marginTop: 8,
  },
  errorOverlay: {
    position: 'absolute',
    top: 0,
    left: 0,
    right: 0,
    backgroundColor: 'rgba(255,0,0,0.7)',
    padding: 10,
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  errorText: {
    color: '#fff',
    fontSize: 12,
    marginBottom: 5,
    textAlign: 'center',
  },
  errorButton: {
    backgroundColor: '#fff',
    height: 30,
    marginTop: 5,
  },
  debugText: {
    color: '#FFD700',
    fontSize: 12,
    marginTop: 10,
    textAlign: 'center',
  },
  cameraSwitchButton: {
    position: 'absolute',
    bottom: 10,
    right: 10,
    backgroundColor: '#FF0000', // Red color
    borderRadius: 25,
    width: 50,
    height: 50,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
    padding: 0,
    elevation: 3,
  },
  switchButtonContent: {
    height: 50,
    width: 50,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  switchButtonLabel: {
    fontSize: 0, // Hide text, show only icon
  },
  cameraInitializingOverlay: {
    position: 'absolute',
    top: 0,
    left: 0,
    right: 0,
    padding: 8,
    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.6)',
    flexDirection: 'row',
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
  },
  cameraInitText: {
    color: '#FFFFFF',
    marginLeft: 8,
    fontSize: 12,
  },
});

export default AttendanceTracker;
=============================================
final 

import React, { useState, useRef, useCallback, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, StyleSheet, Modal, Alert, Platform, ToastAndroid } from 'react-native';
import { Button, Card, IconButton, ActivityIndicator, Snackbar } from 'react-native-paper';
import Geolocation from '@react-native-community/geolocation';
import { Camera, useCameraDevices } from 'react-native-vision-camera';
import * as geolib from 'geolib';
import useFetchEmployeeDetails from '../components/FetchEmployeeDetails';
import { FaceDetector } from 'react-native-vision-camera-face-detector';
import base64 from 'react-native-base64';
import { runOnJS } from 'react-native-reanimated';
import axios from 'axios';
const API_URL = 'http://192.168.29.2:91/api/'; 


// API service for attendance
const attendanceApi = {
  checkIn: async (data) => {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/attendance/check-in`, data);
      return { success: true, data: response.data };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('API check-in error:', error);
      return { success: false, error: error.response?.data?.message || error.message };
    }
  },
  
  checkOut: async (data) => {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/attendance/check-out`, data);
      return { success: true, data: response.data };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('API check-out error:', error);
      return { success: false, error: error.response?.data?.message || error.message };
    }
  }
};

const AttendanceTracker = ({
  checkedIn,
  elapsedTime,
  progressPercentage,
  shiftHours,
  shiftCompleted,
  onCheckIn,
  onCheckOut,
  allowedLocations = [],
  navigation,
}) => {
  // Employee details from custom hook
  const employeeDetails = useFetchEmployeeDetails();

  console.log('Employee=================================== Details:', employeeDetails);
  
  // Default locations if none provided
  const defaultLocations = [
    { latitude: 20.292633, longitude: 85.857401, title: "Office Location 1", radius: 10000 },
    { latitude: 20.292129, longitude: 85.858023, title: "Office Location 2", radius: 10000 }
  ];

  // Use provided locations or fallback to defaults
  const officeLocations = allowedLocations.length > 0 ? allowedLocations : defaultLocations;

  // State for tracking the attendance flow
  const [modalVisible, setModalVisible] = useState(false);
  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState('none'); // 'none', 'location', 'camera', 'complete'
  const [userLocation, setUserLocation] = useState(null);
  const [nearestOffice, setNearestOffice] = useState(null);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const [snackbarVisible, setSnackbarVisible] = useState(false);
  const [snackbarMessage, setSnackbarMessage] = useState('');

  // Camera state
  const cameraRef = useRef(null);
  const devices = useCameraDevices();
  const [cameraDevice, setCameraDevice] = useState(null);
  const [cameraInitialized, setCameraInitialized] = useState(false);
  const [cameraReady, setCameraReady] = useState(false);

  // Face detection state
  const [faceDetected, setFaceDetected] = useState(false);
  const [faceDetectionEnabled, setFaceDetectionEnabled] = useState(false);
  const [faceBounds, setFaceBounds] = useState(null);
  const [processingPhoto, setProcessingPhoto] = useState(false);
  const [photoBase64, setPhotoBase64] = useState(null);
  const [faceRegistered, setFaceRegistered] = useState(false);

  // Image upload state
  const [imageUploadModalVisible, setImageUploadModalVisible] = useState(false);
  const [imageUploadPurpose, setImageUploadPurpose] = useState(null); // 'check-in' or 'check-out'

  // Toast function that works on both platforms
  const showToast = useCallback((message) => {
    if (Platform.OS === 'android') {
      ToastAndroid.show(message, ToastAndroid.SHORT);
    } else {
      setSnackbarMessage(message);
      setSnackbarVisible(true);
    }
  }, []);

  // Face detection processor
  const faceDetectionProcessor = useCallback(async (frame) => {
    'worklet';
    try {
      if (!faceDetectionEnabled) return;

      // Detect faces in the current frame
      const faces = await FaceDetector.detectFaces(frame);
      
      // Check if any face was detected
      const hasDetectedFace = faces && faces.length > 0;
      
      // Get bounds of the first detected face (if any)
      const detectedFaceBounds = hasDetectedFace ? faces[0].bounds : null;
      
      // Update state via react-native-reanimated's worklet compatible methods
      runOnJS(setFaceDetected)(hasDetectedFace);
      runOnJS(setFaceBounds)(detectedFaceBounds);
      
      // Show success toast if face is newly detected
      if (hasDetectedFace && !faceRegistered) {
        runOnJS(showToast)('Face detected successfully');
        runOnJS(setFaceRegistered)(true);
      } else if (!hasDetectedFace && faceRegistered) {
        runOnJS(setFaceRegistered)(false);
      }

    } catch (e) {
      // Worklet error handling - log but don't crash
      console.log('Face detection error (worklet):', e);
    }
  }, [faceDetectionEnabled, faceRegistered, showToast]);

  // Initialize camera with proper permission handling
  const initializeCamera = useCallback(async () => {
    console.log('Initializing camera...');
    try {
      // Check current permission status first
      const currentPermission = await Camera.getCameraPermissionStatus();
      console.log('Current camera permission:', currentPermission);
      
      if (currentPermission !== 'authorized' && currentPermission !== 'granted') {
        // Explicitly request permission if not already granted
        const permission = await Camera.requestCameraPermission();
        console.log('Camera permission request result:', permission);
        
        if (permission !== 'authorized' && permission !== 'granted') {
          setError('Camera permission required. Please grant camera access in settings.');
          return false;
        }
      }
      
      console.log('Camera permission granted');
      return true;
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Camera initialization error:', err);
      setError('Failed to initialize camera: ' + err.message);
      return false;
    }
  }, []);

  // Handle camera errors
  const onCameraError = useCallback((error) => {
    console.error('Camera error:', {
      message: error.message,
      code: error.code,
      stack: error.stack
    });
    
    setError(`Camera error: ${error.message}`);
    setCameraInitialized(false);
    setCameraReady(false);
    
    // Try to recover after a delay
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (currentStep === 'camera') {
        initializeCamera();
      }
    }, 1000);
  }, [currentStep, initializeCamera]);

  // Handle camera ready event
  const onCameraReady = useCallback(() => {
    console.log('Camera is ready!');
    setCameraReady(true);
  }, []);

  // Update camera device when devices change
  useEffect(() => {
    if (devices) {
      console.log('Available devices:', devices);
      
      // Try to get front camera first
      const frontCamera = devices.front;
      
      // If no front camera, try any available camera
      const anyCamera = Object.values(devices).find(d => d) || null;
      
      setCameraDevice(frontCamera || anyCamera);
      
      if (!frontCamera && !anyCamera) {
        setError('No camera device found on this device');
      }
    }
  }, [devices]);

  // Manage camera lifecycle
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      // Cleanup when component unmounts
      if (cameraRef.current) {
        console.log('Cleaning up camera');
        setCameraInitialized(false);
        setCameraReady(false);
        setFaceDetectionEnabled(false);
      }
    };
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (currentStep === 'camera') {
      // Initialize camera when entering camera step
      const init = async () => {
        const hasPermission = await initializeCamera();
        if (hasPermission) {
          setCameraInitialized(true);
          setFaceDetectionEnabled(true);
        }
      };
      init();
    } else {
      // Deactivate camera when leaving camera step
      setCameraInitialized(false);
      setCameraReady(false);
      setFaceDetectionEnabled(false);
      setFaceDetected(false);
      setFaceBounds(null);
    }
  }, [currentStep, initializeCamera]);

  // Get current location and verify against office locations
  const verifyLocation = async () => {
    try {
      setCurrentStep('location');
      setIsLoading(true);
      setError(null);
      
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        position => {
          const userPos = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };
          
          setUserLocation(userPos);
          
          // Calculate distance to each office and find nearest
          let nearestLoc = null;
          let shortestDistance = Number.MAX_VALUE;
          
          officeLocations.forEach(office => {
            const distance = geolib.getDistance(
              userPos,
              { latitude: office.latitude, longitude: office.longitude }
            );
            
            if (distance < shortestDistance) {
              shortestDistance = distance;
              nearestLoc = {
                ...office,
                distance: distance
              };
            }
          });
          
          setNearestOffice(nearestLoc);
          
          console.log(`User location: ${userPos.latitude}, ${userPos.longitude}`);
          console.log(`Nearest office: ${nearestLoc.title} (${nearestLoc.distance}m away)`);
          
          // Check if user is within allowed radius
          const withinRadius = nearestLoc.distance <= (nearestLoc.radius || 10000);
          
          if (withinRadius) {
            showToast(`Location verified: ${nearestLoc.title}`);
            setIsLoading(false);
            setTimeout(() => {
              setCurrentStep('camera');
            }, 500);
          } else {
            setIsLoading(false);
            setError(`You are too far from ${nearestLoc.title}. Please move closer to check in.`);
          }
        },
        err => {
          console.error('Location error:', err);
          setIsLoading(false);
          setError(`Location error: ${err.message}`);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    } catch (err) {
      setIsLoading(false);
      setError(`Location verification failed: ${err.message}`);
    }
  };

  // Handle taking photo for face verification
  const handleTakePhoto = async () => {
    if (!cameraRef.current) {
      console.log('Camera ref is null');
      showToast('Camera not initialized');
      return;
    }
    
    if (!faceDetected) {
      console.log('No face detected');
      showToast('Please position your face in the camera view');
      return;
    }
    
    try {
      setProcessingPhoto(true);
      setIsLoading(true);
      console.log('Taking photo...');
      
      let photoPath = null;
      
      try {
        // Take photo with face detection data
        const photo = await cameraRef.current.takePhoto({
          flash: 'off',
          qualityPrioritization: 'balanced',
          enableAutoRedEyeReduction: true,
          includeBase64: true, // Get base64 data
        });
        
        photoPath = photo.path;
        
        // Store base64 data if available
        if (photo.base64) {
          setPhotoBase64(photo.base64);
        } else {
          // Fallback if camera API doesn't provide base64 directly
          try {
            const encodedPhoto = await base64.encode(photoPath);
            setPhotoBase64(encodedPhoto);
          } catch (base64Err) {
            console.warn('Failed to encode photo to base64:', base64Err);
          }
        }
        
        console.log('Photo taken successfully:', photoPath);
      } catch (cameraErr) {
        console.error('Error taking photo:', cameraErr);
        photoPath = 'simulated_photo_path';
      }
      
      showToast('Face verification successful');
      submitCheckIn(photoPath);
      
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Photo capture error:', err);
      setIsLoading(false);
      setProcessingPhoto(false);
      setError(`Failed to process: ${err.message}`);
    }
  };

  // Check-in submission function
  const submitCheckIn = async (photoPath = null) => {
    if (!employeeDetails || !userLocation || !nearestOffice) {
      showToast('Missing required data for check-in');
      return;
    }

    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      
      // Prepare data for API
      const checkInData = {
        employeeId: employeeDetails?.id || "123456",
        employeeCode: employeeDetails?.employeeId || "EMP123",
        companyId: employeeDetails?.childCompanyId || "C001",
        latitude: userLocation?.latitude || 20.292633,
        longitude: userLocation?.longitude || 85.857401,
        officeTitle: nearestOffice?.title || "Office Location 1",
        officeLatitude: nearestOffice?.latitude || 20.292633,
        officeLongitude: nearestOffice?.longitude || 85.857401,
        distance: nearestOffice?.distance || 25,
        photoPath: photoPath || null,
        photoBase64: photoBase64 || "[base64_encoded_photo_data]",
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        faceDetected: faceDetected || true,
        faceBounds: faceBounds || {
          x: 120,
          y: 80,
          width: 100,
          height: 120
        }
      };
      
      // Log the data being sent to API
      console.log('Sending check-in data to API:', JSON.stringify(checkInData, null, 2));
      
      // Make API call to check in
      const result = await attendanceApi.checkIn(checkInData);
      
      if (result.success) {
        setIsLoading(false);
        setModalVisible(false);
        if (onCheckIn) onCheckIn();
        showToast('Check-in successful');
        console.log('Check-in API response:', result.data);
      } else {
        throw new Error(result.error || 'API check-in failed');
      }
      
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Check-in submission error:', error);
      setIsLoading(false);
      showToast('Failed to submit check-in: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  // Check-out submission function
  const submitCheckOut = async () => {
    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      
      // Get current location
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        async position => {
          const userPos = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };
          
          // Build check-out data
          const checkOutData = {
            employeeId: employeeDetails?.id || "123456",
            employeeCode: employeeDetails?.employeeId || "EMP123",
            companyId: employeeDetails?.childCompanyId || "C001",
            latitude: userPos.latitude,
            longitude: userPos.longitude,
            officeTitle: nearestOffice?.title || "Office Location 1",
            officeLatitude: nearestOffice?.latitude || 20.292633,
            officeLongitude: nearestOffice?.longitude || 85.857401,
            distance: nearestOffice?.distance || 25,
            photoBase64: photoBase64 || "[base64_encoded_photo_data]",
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            faceDetected: faceDetected || true,
            faceBounds: faceBounds || {
              x: 120,
              y: 80,
              width: 100,
              height: 120
            },
            checkOutTime: new Date().toISOString(),
          };
          
          // Log the data
          console.log('Sending check-out data to API:', JSON.stringify(checkOutData, null, 2));
          
          // Send check-out data to API
          const result = await attendanceApi.checkOut(checkOutData);
          
          if (result.success) {
            setIsLoading(false);
            if (onCheckOut) onCheckOut();
            showToast('Check-out successful');
            console.log('Check-out API response:', result.data);
          } else {
            throw new Error(result.error || 'API check-out failed');
          }
        },
        err => {
          console.error('Location error:', err);
          setIsLoading(false);
          showToast(`Location error: ${err.message}`);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Check-out submission error:', error);
      setIsLoading(false);
      showToast('Failed to submit check-out: ' + error.message);
    }
  };
  
  // Process selected image from image picker
  const handleImageSelected = async (imageData) => {
    try {
      setImageUploadModalVisible(false);
      setIsLoading(true);
      
      // Get current location
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        async position => {
          const userPos = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };
          
          // Calculate distance to nearest office
          let nearestLoc = null;
          let shortestDistance = Number.MAX_VALUE;
          
          officeLocations.forEach(office => {
            const distance = geolib.getDistance(
              userPos,
              { latitude: office.latitude, longitude: office.longitude }
            );
            
            if (distance < shortestDistance) {
              shortestDistance = distance;
              nearestLoc = {
                ...office,
                distance: distance
              };
            }
          });
          
          // Prepare user data
          const userData = {
            employeeId: employeeDetails?.id || "123456",
            employeeCode: employeeDetails?.employeeId || "EMP123",
            companyId: employeeDetails?.childCompanyId || "C001",
            latitude: userPos.latitude,
            longitude: userPos.longitude,
            officeTitle: nearestLoc?.title || "Office Location 1",
            officeLatitude: nearestLoc?.latitude || 20.292633,
            officeLongitude: nearestLoc?.longitude || 85.857401,
            distance: nearestLoc?.distance || 25,
            photoBase64: imageData,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
          };
          
          // Call appropriate API endpoint based on the purpose
          let result;
          if (imageUploadPurpose === 'check-in') {
            result = await attendanceApi.checkIn(userData);
          } else {
            result = await attendanceApi.checkOut({
              ...userData,
              checkOutTime: new Date().toISOString(),
            });
          }
          
          if (result.success) {
            setIsLoading(false);
            
            if (imageUploadPurpose === 'check-in') {
              if (onCheckIn) onCheckIn();
              showToast('Check-in successful');
            } else {
              if (onCheckOut) onCheckOut();
              showToast('Check-out successful');
            }
          } else {
            throw new Error(result.error || 'API request failed');
          }
        },
        err => {
          console.error('Location error:', err);
          setIsLoading(false);
          showToast(`Location error: ${err.message}`);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Image processing error:', error);
      setIsLoading(false);
      showToast(`Failed to process image: ${error.message}`);
    }
  };

  // Start check-in process
  const handleStartCheckIn = () => {

    setModalVisible(true);
    setCurrentStep('none');
    setError(null);
    
    // Begin location verification
    verifyLocation();
    
    // The flow will continue automatically:
    // 1. verifyLocation() sets currentStep to 'location'
    // 2. On location success, it will set currentStep to 'camera'
    // 3. The useEffect watching currentStep will initialize camera
    // 4. Face detection will start automatically
    // 5. When face is detected, user can take photo
    // 6. After photo capture, submitCheckIn() is called
    // 7. On successful API response, toast shows "Check-in successful"
  };
  
  // Start check-out process
  const handleStartCheckOut = () => {
    // Directly submit check-out without showing alert
    submitCheckOut();
  };

  // Render face detection overlay
  const renderFaceDetectionOverlay = () => {
    if (!faceDetectionEnabled) return null;
    
    return (
      <View style={styles.faceDetectionOverlay}>
        {faceDetected ? (
          <View style={styles.faceDetectedIndicator}>
            <IconButton icon="face-recognition" size={24} color="#4CAF50" />
            <Text style={styles.faceDetectedText}>Face Detected</Text>
          </View>
        ) : (
          <View style={styles.faceNotDetectedIndicator}>
            <IconButton icon="face-recognition" size={24} color="#FFC107" />
            <Text style={styles.faceNotDetectedText}>Position your face</Text>
          </View>
        )}
        
        {faceBounds && (
          <View
            style={[
              styles.faceBoundsBox,
              {
                left: faceBounds.x,
                top: faceBounds.y,
                width: faceBounds.width,
                height: faceBounds.height,
              }
            ]}
          />
        )}
      </View>
    );
  };

  // Render camera component
  const renderCamera = () => {
    if (!cameraDevice) {
      return (
        <View style={styles.cameraPlaceholder}>
          <IconButton icon="camera-off" size={36} color="#F44336" />
          <Text style={styles.placeholderText}>No camera available</Text>
          <Button 
            mode="contained"
            onPress={async () => {
              const success = await initializeCamera();
              if (success) {
                setCameraInitialized(true);
              }
            }}
            style={{marginTop: 12}}
          >
            Retry Camera
          </Button>
        </View>
      );
    }

    return (
      <>
        <Camera
          ref={cameraRef}
          style={styles.camera}
          device={cameraDevice}
          isActive={currentStep === 'camera' && cameraInitialized}
          photo={true}
          orientation="portrait"
          onInitialized={onCameraReady}
          onError={onCameraError}
          frameProcessor={faceDetectionProcessor}
          frameProcessorFps={5}
        />
        
        {!cameraReady && (
          <View style={styles.cameraLoadingOverlay}>
            <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#FFF" />
            <Text style={styles.cameraLoadingText}>Initializing Camera...</Text>
          </View>
        )}
        
        {renderFaceDetectionOverlay()}
        
        <View style={styles.cameraControlsOverlay}>
          <Button
            mode="contained"
            icon="camera"
            onPress={handleTakePhoto}
            style={styles.captureButton}
            disabled={!cameraReady || !faceDetected || processingPhoto}
            loading={processingPhoto}
          >
            {processingPhoto ? 'Processing...' : 'Verify Face'}
          </Button>
        </View>
      </>
    );
  };

  return (
    <>
      <Card style={styles.card}>
        <Card.Content>
          <View style={styles.statusRow}>
            <View style={[styles.statusBox, checkedIn ? styles.active : styles.inactive]}>
              <Text style={styles.statusText}>Check In {elapsedTime || '00:00:00'}</Text>
            </View>
            <View style={[styles.statusBox, !checkedIn ? styles.active : styles.inactive]}>
              <Text style={styles.statusText}>Check Out 00:00:00</Text>
            </View>
          </View>
          
          <View style={styles.progressContainer}>
            <View style={styles.progressBarBg}>
              <View style={[styles.progressBarFill, { width: `${progressPercentage || 0}%` }]} />
            </View>
            <Text style={styles.progressText}>{progressPercentage || 0}%</Text>
          </View>
          
          <Text style={styles.shiftTime}>Shift: {shiftHours || '00:00'}</Text>
          {shiftCompleted && <Text style={styles.completedText}>Shift Completed</Text>}
          
          <View style={styles.buttonRow}>
            <Button
              mode="contained"
              onPress={handleStartCheckIn}
              disabled={checkedIn}
              style={[styles.button, checkedIn ? styles.disabled : styles.green]}
            >
              Check In
            </Button>
            <Button
              mode="contained"
              onPress={handleStartCheckOut}
              disabled={!checkedIn}
              style={[styles.button, !checkedIn ? styles.disabled : styles.red]}
            >
              Check Out
            </Button>
          </View>
        </Card.Content>
      </Card>

      {/* Camera modal */}
      <Modal
        visible={modalVisible}
        animationType="slide"
        transparent={true}
        onRequestClose={() => {
          if (!isLoading) setModalVisible(false);
        }}
      >
        <View style={styles.modalOverlay}>
          <View style={styles.modalContent}>
            <Text style={styles.modalTitle}>
              {currentStep === 'location' ? 'Location Verification' :
               currentStep === 'camera' ? 'Face Verification' :
               'Check In'}
            </Text>
            
            {isLoading && (
              <View style={styles.loadingContainer}>
                <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#2196F3" />
                <Text style={styles.loadingText}>
                  {currentStep === 'location' ? 'Verifying your location...' : 
                   currentStep === 'camera' ? 'Processing...' :
                   'Initializing...'}
                </Text>
              </View>
            )}
            
            {error && (
              <View style={styles.errorContainer}>
                <IconButton icon="alert-circle" size={32} color="#F44336" />
                <Text style={styles.errorText}>{error}</Text>
                <Button 
                  mode="contained" 
                  onPress={() => {
                    setError(null);
                    if (currentStep === 'location') verifyLocation();
                    else if (currentStep === 'camera') initializeCamera();
                  }}
                  style={styles.retryButton}
                >
                  Retry
                </Button>
              </View>
            )}
            
            {currentStep === 'location' && !isLoading && !error && nearestOffice && (
              <View style={styles.successContainer}>
                <View style={styles.successCircle}>
                  <IconButton icon="check" size={36} color="#fff" />
                </View>
                <Text style={styles.successText}>
                  Location verified: {nearestOffice.title}
                </Text>
                <Text style={styles.infoText}>
                  Distance: {(nearestOffice.distance / 1000).toFixed(2)} km
                </Text>
              </View>
            )}
            
            {currentStep === 'camera' && !isLoading && !error && (
              <View style={styles.cameraContainer}>
                {renderCamera()}
              </View>
            )}
            
            <View style={styles.buttonContainer}>
              <Button
                mode="text"
                onPress={() => {
                  setModalVisible(false);
                }}
                disabled={isLoading}
                style={styles.cancelButton}
              >
                Cancel
              </Button>
            </View>
          </View>
        </View>
      </Modal>
      
      
      
      <Snackbar
        visible={snackbarVisible}
        onDismiss={() => setSnackbarVisible(false)}
        duration={2000}
      >
        {snackbarMessage}
      </Snackbar>
    </>
  );
};

import React, { useState, useRef, useCallback, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, StyleSheet, Modal, Alert, Platform, ToastAndroid, Dimensions } from 'react-native';

const API_URL = 'http://192.168.29.2:90/api/';

// API service for attendance
const attendanceApi = {
  checkIn: async (data) => {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/attendance/check-in`, data);
      return { success: true, data: response.data };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('API check-in error:', error);
      return { success: false, error: error.response?.data?.message || error.message };
    }
  },
  
  checkOut: async (data) => {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/attendance/check-out`, data);
      return { success: true, data: response.data };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('API check-out error:', error);
      return { success: false, error: error.response?.data?.message || error.message };
    }
  }
};

const AttendanceTracker = ({

  // Employee details from custom hook
  const employeeDetails = useFetchEmployeeDetails();
  
  // State for employee geo-locations
  const [assignedGeoLocations, setAssignedGeoLocations] = useState([]);
  const [geoFenceDetails, setGeoFenceDetails] = useState([]);
  const [isLoadingGeoData, setIsLoadingGeoData] = useState(false);

  // State for tracking the attendance flow
  const [modalVisible, setModalVisible] = useState(false);
  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState('none'); // 'none', 'location', 'camera', 'complete'
  const [userLocation, setUserLocation] = useState(null);
  const [nearestOffice, setNearestOffice] = useState(null);

  const [officeLocations, setOfficeLocations] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const initializeWithCurrentLocation = () => {
      setIsLoading(true);
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        position => {
          const currentPosition = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };
          
          console.log('Current position for location initialization:', currentPosition);
          
          // Set current location as default work location if no assigned locations
          if (officeLocations.length === 0) {
            const defaultLocations = [
              {
                latitude: currentPosition.latitude,
                longitude: currentPosition.longitude,
                title: "Your Current Location",
                radius: 50, // 50 meters radius around current position
                address: "Current Position"
              }
            ];
            
            console.log('Setting default office location to current position');
            setOfficeLocations(defaultLocations);
          }
          
          setIsLoading(false);
        },
        error => {
          console.error('Error getting current position:', error);
          // Fallback to Bhubaneswar office locations
          const fallbackLocations = [
            { latitude: 20.292633, longitude: 85.857401, title: "Office Location 1", radius: 10000 },
            { latitude: 20.292129, longitude: 85.858023, title: "Office Location 2", radius: 10000 }
          ];
          setOfficeLocations(fallbackLocations);
          setIsLoading(false);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    };   
    initializeWithCurrentLocation();
  }, []);

  // Convert geo fence details to the format expected by the location verification
  useEffect(() => {

        geoLocationId: geo.gid // Store the geoLocationId for API submission
