  // Camera state
  const cameraRef = useRef(null);
  const devices = useCameraDevices();
  const [cameraDevice, setCameraDevice] = useState(null);
  const [cameraInitialized, setCameraInitialized] = useState(false);
  const [cameraReady, setCameraReady] = useState(false);

  // Face detection state
  const [faceDetected, setFaceDetected] = useState(false);
  const [faceDetectionEnabled, setFaceDetectionEnabled] = useState(false);
  const [faceBounds, setFaceBounds] = useState(null);
  const [processingPhoto, setProcessingPhoto] = useState(false);
  const [photoBase64, setPhotoBase64] = useState(null);
  const [faceRegistered, setFaceRegistered] = useState(false);

  // Image upload state
  const [imageUploadModalVisible, setImageUploadModalVisible] = useState(false);
  const [imageUploadPurpose, setImageUploadPurpose] = useState(null); // 'check-in' or 'check-out'

  // Toast function that works on both platforms
  const showToast = useCallback((message) => {
    if (Platform.OS === 'android') {
      ToastAndroid.show(message, ToastAndroid.SHORT);
    } else {
      setSnackbarMessage(message);
      setSnackbarVisible(true);
    }
  }, []);

  // Face detection processor
  const faceDetectionProcessor = useCallback(async (frame) => {
    'worklet';
    try {
      if (!faceDetectionEnabled) return;

      // Detect faces in the current frame
      const faces = await FaceDetector.detectFaces(frame);
      
      // Check if any face was detected
      const hasDetectedFace = faces && faces.length > 0;
      
      // Get bounds of the first detected face (if any)
      const detectedFaceBounds = hasDetectedFace ? faces[0].bounds : null;
      
      // Update state via react-native-reanimated's worklet compatible methods
      runOnJS(setFaceDetected)(hasDetectedFace);
      runOnJS(setFaceBounds)(detectedFaceBounds);
      
      // Show success toast if face is newly detected
      if (hasDetectedFace && !faceRegistered) {
        runOnJS(showToast)('Face detected successfully');
        runOnJS(setFaceRegistered)(true);
      } else if (!hasDetectedFace && faceRegistered) {
        runOnJS(setFaceRegistered)(false);
      }

    } catch (e) {
      // Worklet error handling - log but don't crash
      console.log('Face detection error (worklet):', e);
    }
  }, [faceDetectionEnabled, faceRegistered, showToast]);

  // Initialize camera with proper permission handling
  const initializeCamera = useCallback(async () => {
    console.log('Initializing camera...');
    try {
      // Check current permission status first
      const currentPermission = await Camera.getCameraPermissionStatus();
      console.log('Current camera permission:', currentPermission);
      
      if (currentPermission !== 'authorized' && currentPermission !== 'granted') {
        // Explicitly request permission if not already granted
        const permission = await Camera.requestCameraPermission();
        console.log('Camera permission request result:', permission);
        
        if (permission !== 'authorized' && permission !== 'granted') {
          setError('Camera permission required. Please grant camera access in settings.');
          return false;
        }
      }
      
      console.log('Camera permission granted');
      return true;
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Camera initialization error:', err);
      setError('Failed to initialize camera: ' + err.message);
      return false;
    }
  }, []);

  // Handle camera errors
  const onCameraError = useCallback((error) => {
    console.error('Camera error:', {
      message: error.message,
      code: error.code,
      stack: error.stack
    });
    
    setError(`Camera error: ${error.message}`);
    setCameraInitialized(false);
    setCameraReady(false);
    
    // Try to recover after a delay
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (currentStep === 'camera') {
        initializeCamera();
      }
    }, 1000);
  }, [currentStep, initializeCamera]);

  // Handle camera ready event
  const onCameraReady = useCallback(() => {
    console.log('Camera is ready!');
    setCameraReady(true);
  }, []);

  // Update camera device when devices change
  useEffect(() => {
    if (devices) {
      console.log('Available devices:', devices);
      
      // Try to get front camera first
      const frontCamera = devices.front;
      
      // If no front camera, try any available camera
      const anyCamera = Object.values(devices).find(d => d) || null;
      
      setCameraDevice(frontCamera || anyCamera);
      
      if (!frontCamera && !anyCamera) {
        setError('No camera device found on this device');
      }
    }
  }, [devices]);

  // Manage camera lifecycle
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      // Cleanup when component unmounts
      if (cameraRef.current) {
        console.log('Cleaning up camera');
        setCameraInitialized(false);
        setCameraReady(false);
        setFaceDetectionEnabled(false);
      }
    };
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (currentStep === 'camera') {
      // Initialize camera when entering camera step
      const init = async () => {
        const hasPermission = await initializeCamera();
        if (hasPermission) {
          setCameraInitialized(true);
          setFaceDetectionEnabled(true);
        }
      };
      init();
    } else {
      // Deactivate camera when leaving camera step
      setCameraInitialized(false);
      setCameraReady(false);
      setFaceDetectionEnabled(false);
      setFaceDetected(false);
      setFaceBounds(null);
    }
  }, [currentStep, initializeCamera]);

  // Fetch assigned geo locations for current employee
  const fetchAssignedGeoLocations = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!employeeDetails?.id) {
      console.log('No employee ID available to fetch geo locations');
      return;
    }

    try {
      setIsLoadingGeoData(true);
      console.log(`Fetching assigned geo locations for employee ${employeeDetails.id}`);
      
      const response = await axios.get(
        `${API_URL}GeoFencing/getAssignedGeoLocationIdsByEmployeeId/${employeeDetails.id}/${employeeDetails.childCompanyId}`
      );
      
      console.log('API RESPONSE - ASSIGNED GEO LOCATIONS:');
      console.log('===========================================');
      console.log(JSON.stringify(response.data, null, 2));
      console.log('===========================================');
      
      setAssignedGeoLocations(response.data);
      
      // For each assigned geo location, fetch its details
      if (response.data && response.data.length > 0) {
        const fetchedGeoDetails = [];
        
        for (const assignedGeo of response.data) {
          const geoId = assignedGeo.geoLocationId;
          try {
            console.log(`Fetching geo fence details for ID: ${geoId}`);
            const geoDetailsResponse = await axios.get(
              `${API_URL}GeoFencing/GetGeoFenceDetails/${geoId}`
            );
            
            console.log('API RESPONSE - GEO FENCE DETAILS:');
            console.log('===========================================');
            console.log(JSON.stringify(geoDetailsResponse.data, null, 2));
            console.log('===========================================');
            
            fetchedGeoDetails.push(geoDetailsResponse.data);
          } catch (error) {
            console.error(`Error fetching geo fence details for ID ${geoId}:`, error);
            console.error('Error response:', error.response?.data);
          }
        }
        
        setGeoFenceDetails(fetchedGeoDetails);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching assigned geo locations:', error);
      console.error('Error response:', error.response?.data);
    } finally {
      setIsLoadingGeoData(false);
    }
  }, [employeeDetails?.id, employeeDetails?.childCompanyId]);
  
  // Fetch geo locations when employee details are loaded
  useEffect(() => {
    if (employeeDetails?.id) {
      fetchAssignedGeoLocations();
    }
  }, [employeeDetails, fetchAssignedGeoLocations]);

  // Convert geo fence details to the format expected by the location verification
  useEffect(() => {
    if (geoFenceDetails.length > 0) {
      const convertedLocations = geoFenceDetails.map(geo => ({
        latitude: parseFloat(geo.lattitude),
        longitude: parseFloat(geo.longitude),
        title: geo.geoLocationName,
        radius: parseFloat(geo.radius) * 1000, // Convert radius to meters
        address: geo.address,
        areaType: geo.areaType,
        geoLocationId: geo.gid // Store the geoLocationId for API submission
      }));
      
      console.log('GEO LOCATIONS DETAILS:');
      console.log('===========================================');
      convertedLocations.forEach((loc, idx) => {
        console.log(`[${idx+1}] ${loc.title}:`);
        console.log(`  - Coordinates: ${loc.latitude}, ${loc.longitude}`);
        console.log(`  - Radius: ${loc.radius} meters`);
        console.log(`  - ID: ${loc.geoLocationId}`);
        console.log(`  - Area Type: ${loc.areaType}`);
      });
      console.log('===========================================');
      
      // Replace default locations with assigned locations
      if (convertedLocations.length > 0) {
        setOfficeLocations(convertedLocations);
      }
    }
  }, [geoFenceDetails]);


  const handleTakePhoto = async () => {
    if (!cameraRef.current) {
      console.log('Camera ref is null');
      showToast('Camera not initialized');
      return;
    }
    
    if (!faceDetected) {
      console.log('No face detected');
      showToast('Please position your face in the camera view');
      return;
    }
    
    try {
      setProcessingPhoto(true);
      setIsLoading(true);
      console.log('Taking photo...');
      
      let photoPath = null;
      
      try {
        // Take photo with face detection data
        const photo = await cameraRef.current.takePhoto({
          flash: 'off',
          qualityPrioritization: 'balanced',
          enableAutoRedEyeReduction: true,
          includeBase64: true, // Get base64 data
        });
        
        photoPath = photo.path;
        
        // Store base64 data if available
        if (photo.base64) {
          setPhotoBase64(photo.base64);
        } else {
          // Fallback if camera API doesn't provide base64 directly
          try {
            const encodedPhoto = await base64.encode(photoPath);
            setPhotoBase64(encodedPhoto);
          } catch (base64Err) {
            console.warn('Failed to encode photo to base64:', base64Err);
          }
        }
        
        console.log('Photo taken successfully:', photoPath);
      } catch (cameraErr) {
        console.error('Error taking photo:', cameraErr);
        photoPath = 'simulated_photo_path';
      }
      
      showToast('Face verification successful');
      submitCheckIn(photoPath);
      
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Photo capture error:', err);
      setIsLoading(false);
      setProcessingPhoto(false);
      setError(`Failed to process: ${err.message}`);
    }
  };

  // Check-in submission function
  const submitCheckIn = async (photoPath = null) => {
    // Wait for employee details if not available yet
    if (!employeeDetails) {
      console.log('Waiting for employee details before check-in...');
      setTimeout(() => submitCheckIn(photoPath), 1000);
      return;
    }
    
    if (!userLocation || !nearestOffice) {
      showToast('Missing location data for check-in');
      console.error('Missing required data for check-in:');
      console.error('User location:', userLocation);
      console.error('Nearest office:', nearestOffice);
      return;
    }

    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      
      // Log the detailed data for check-in
      console.log('CHECK-IN SUBMISSION - DETAILED LOG');
      console.log('===========================================');
      console.log('Employee details:', {
        id: employeeDetails.id,
        employeeId: employeeDetails.employeeId,
        name: employeeDetails.employeeName,
        companyId: employeeDetails.childCompanyId
      });
      
      console.log('Location data:', {
        userLocation: userLocation,
        nearestOffice: nearestOffice,
        distance: nearestOffice.distance,
        withinRadius: nearestOffice.distance <= nearestOffice.radius
      });
      
      console.log('Face detection data:', {
        faceDetected: faceDetected,
        faceBounds: faceBounds
      });
      console.log('===========================================');
      
      // Prepare data for API with geo location details
      const checkInData = {
        employeeId: employeeDetails.id,
        employeeCode: employeeDetails.employeeId,
        companyId: employeeDetails.childCompanyId,
        latitude: userLocation?.latitude,
        longitude: userLocation?.longitude,
        officeTitle: nearestOffice?.title,
        officeLatitude: nearestOffice?.latitude,
        officeLongitude: nearestOffice?.longitude,
        distance: nearestOffice?.distance,
        photoPath: photoPath || null,
        photoBase64: photoBase64 || "[base64_encoded_photo_data]",
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        faceDetected: faceDetected,
        faceBounds: faceBounds,
        geoLocationId: nearestOffice.geoLocationId || null,
        areaType: nearestOffice.areaType || null
      };
      
      // Log the data being sent to API
      console.log('Sending check-in data to API:', JSON.stringify(checkInData, null, 2));
      
      // Make API call to check in
      const result = await attendanceApi.checkIn(checkInData);
      
      if (result.success) {
        setIsLoading(false);
        setModalVisible(false);
        if (onCheckIn) onCheckIn();
        showToast('Check-in successful');
        console.log('Check-in API response:', result.data);
      } else {
        throw new Error(result.error || 'API check-in failed');
      }
      
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Check-in submission error:', error);
      setIsLoading(false);
      showToast('Failed to submit check-in: ' + error.message);
    }
  };

  // Check-out submission function
  const submitCheckOut = async () => {
    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      
      // Get current location
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        async position => {
          const userPos = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };
          
          // Build check-out data
          const checkOutData = {
            employeeId: employeeDetails?.id || "123456",
            employeeCode: employeeDetails?.employeeId || "EMP123",
            companyId: employeeDetails?.childCompanyId || "C001",
            latitude: userPos.latitude,
            longitude: userPos.longitude,
            officeTitle: nearestOffice?.title || "Office Location 1",
            officeLatitude: nearestOffice?.latitude || 20.292633,
            officeLongitude: nearestOffice?.longitude || 85.857401,
            distance: nearestOffice?.distance || 25,
            photoBase64: photoBase64 || "[base64_encoded_photo_data]",
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            faceDetected: faceDetected || true,
            faceBounds: faceBounds || {
              x: 120,
              y: 80,
              width: 100,
              height: 120
            },
            checkOutTime: new Date().toISOString(),
          };
          
          // Log the data
          console.log('Sending check-out data to API:', JSON.stringify(checkOutData, null, 2));
          
          // Send check-out data to API
          const result = await attendanceApi.checkOut(checkOutData);
          
          if (result.success) {
            setIsLoading(false);
            if (onCheckOut) onCheckOut();
            showToast('Check-out successful');
            console.log('Check-out API response:', result.data);
          } else {
            throw new Error(result.error || 'API check-out failed');
          }
        },
        err => {
          console.error('Location error:', err);
          setIsLoading(false);
          showToast(`Location error: ${err.message}`);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Check-out submission error:', error);
      setIsLoading(false);
      showToast('Failed to submit check-out: ' + error.message);
    }
  };
  
  // Process selected image from image picker
  const handleImageSelected = async (imageData) => {
    try {
      setImageUploadModalVisible(false);
      setIsLoading(true);
      
      // Get current location
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        async position => {
          const userPos = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };
          
          // Calculate distance to nearest office
          let nearestLoc = null;
          let shortestDistance = Number.MAX_VALUE;
          
          officeLocations.forEach(office => {
            const distance = geolib.getDistance(
              userPos,
              { latitude: office.latitude, longitude: office.longitude }
            );
            
            if (distance < shortestDistance) {
              shortestDistance = distance;
              nearestLoc = {
                ...office,
                distance: distance
              };
            }
          });
          
          // Prepare user data
          const userData = {
            employeeId: employeeDetails?.id || "123456",
            employeeCode: employeeDetails?.employeeId || "EMP123",
            companyId: employeeDetails?.childCompanyId || "C001",
            latitude: userPos.latitude,
            longitude: userPos.longitude,
            officeTitle: nearestLoc?.title || "Office Location 1",
            officeLatitude: nearestLoc?.latitude || 20.292633,
            officeLongitude: nearestLoc?.longitude || 85.857401,
            distance: nearestLoc?.distance || 25,
            photoBase64: imageData,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
          };
          
          // Call appropriate API endpoint based on the purpose
          let result;
          if (imageUploadPurpose === 'check-in') {
            result = await attendanceApi.checkIn(userData);
          } else {
            result = await attendanceApi.checkOut({
              ...userData,
              checkOutTime: new Date().toISOString(),
            });
          }
          
          if (result.success) {
            setIsLoading(false);
            
            if (imageUploadPurpose === 'check-in') {
              if (onCheckIn) onCheckIn();
              showToast('Check-in successful');
            } else {
              if (onCheckOut) onCheckOut();
              showToast('Check-out successful');
            }
          } else {
            throw new Error(result.error || 'API request failed');
          }
        },
        err => {
          console.error('Location error:', err);
          setIsLoading(false);
          showToast(`Location error: ${err.message}`);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Image processing error:', error);
      setIsLoading(false);
      showToast(`Failed to process image: ${error.message}`);
    }
  };

  // Start check-in process
  const handleStartCheckIn = () => {
    setModalVisible(true);
    setCurrentStep('none');
    setError(null);
    
    // Begin location verification with map
    verifyLocationWithMap();
  };

  // Start check-out process
  const handleStartCheckOut = () => {
    // Directly submit check-out without showing alert
    submitCheckOut();
  };

  // Initialize map with current location
  const initializeMap = useCallback((currentPosition) => {
    if (!currentPosition) return;
    
    const newRegion = {
      latitude: currentPosition.latitude,
      longitude: currentPosition.longitude,
      latitudeDelta: 0.005, // Zoom level
      longitudeDelta: 0.005,
    };
    
    setRegion(newRegion);
  }, []);

  // Enhanced location verification function with map display
  const verifyLocationWithMap = () => {
    try {
      setCurrentStep('location');
      setIsLoading(true);
      setError(null);
      setMapVisible(true);
      
      // If no office locations defined yet, display error
      if (officeLocations.length === 0) {
        console.log('No office locations defined yet');
        setError('No office locations defined. Please try again.');
        setIsLoading(false);
        return;
      }
      
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        position => {
          const userPos = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };
          
          console.log('===========================================');
          console.log('LOCATION VERIFICATION - DETAILED LOG');
          console.log('===========================================');
          console.log(`User current position: ${JSON.stringify(userPos)}`);
          
          setUserLocation(userPos);
          initializeMap(userPos);
          
          // Calculate distance to each office and find nearest
          let nearestLoc = null;
          let shortestDistance = Number.MAX_VALUE;
          let isWithinAnyOffice = false;
          
          console.log('Available office locations:');
          officeLocations.forEach((office, index) => {
            const distance = geolib.getDistance(
              userPos,
              { latitude: office.latitude, longitude: office.longitude }
            );
            
            // Check if user is within this office radius
            const withinThisOffice = distance <= office.radius;
            if (withinThisOffice) {
              isWithinAnyOffice = true;
            }
            
            // Calculate the percentage of similarity between coordinates (for close matches)
            const latSimilarity = (1 - Math.abs((userPos.latitude - office.latitude) / office.latitude)) * 100;
            const lngSimilarity = (1 - Math.abs((userPos.longitude - office.longitude) / office.longitude)) * 100;
            const coordSimilarity = (latSimilarity + lngSimilarity) / 2;
            
            console.log(`[${index+1}] ${office.title}:`);
            console.log(`  - API coordinates: ${office.latitude}, ${office.longitude}`);
            console.log(`  - User coordinates: ${userPos.latitude}, ${userPos.longitude}`);
            console.log(`  - Coordinate similarity: ${coordSimilarity.toFixed(2)}%`);
            console.log(`  - Distance: ${distance} meters`);
            console.log(`  - Allowed radius: ${office.radius} meters`);
            console.log(`  - Within radius: ${withinThisOffice ? 'YES' : 'NO'}`);
            
            if (distance < shortestDistance) {
              shortestDistance = distance;
              nearestLoc = {
                ...office,
                distance: distance,
                geoLocationId: office.geoLocationId || (assignedGeoLocations[index]?.geoLocationId || null),
                coordSimilarity: coordSimilarity
              };
            }
          });
          
          setNearestOffice(nearestLoc);
          
          console.log('===========================================');
          console.log('LOCATION MATCH RESULT:');
          console.log(`- Nearest office: ${nearestLoc.title}`);
          console.log(`- API coordinates: ${nearestLoc.latitude}, ${nearestLoc.longitude}`);
          console.log(`- User coordinates: ${userPos.latitude}, ${userPos.longitude}`);
          console.log(`- Distance: ${nearestLoc.distance} meters`);
          console.log(`- Coordinate similarity: ${nearestLoc.coordSimilarity.toFixed(2)}%`);
          
          // Check if user is within allowed radius of the nearest office
          const withinRadius = nearestLoc.distance <= nearestLoc.radius;
          console.log(`- Location match success: ${withinRadius ? 'YES' : 'NO'}`);
          
          if (withinRadius) {
            console.log('‚úÖ SUCCESS: Current location matches office location within allowed radius!');
            console.log(`‚úÖ User is inside ${nearestLoc.title} geofence (${nearestLoc.distance}m from center)`);
          } else {
            console.log('‚ùå FAILED: Current location does not match any office location');
            console.log(`‚ùå User is ${nearestLoc.distance}m away from ${nearestLoc.title}, outside the ${nearestLoc.radius}m radius`); 
          }
          console.log('===========================================');
          
          setTimeout(() => {
            setIsLoading(false);
            
            if (withinRadius) {
              showToast(`Location verified: ${nearestLoc.title}`);
              // Automatically proceed to next step after showing the map for a moment
              setTimeout(() => {
                setMapVisible(false);
                setCurrentStep('camera');
              }, 2000);
            } else {
              // Show alert for location mismatch
              Alert.alert(
                "Location Verification Failed",
                `You are ${(nearestLoc.distance/1000).toFixed(2)} km away from ${nearestLoc.title}. You need to be within ${(nearestLoc.radius/1000).toFixed(2)} km radius to check in.`,
                [
                  {
                    text: "Try Again",
                    onPress: () => verifyLocationWithMap()
                  },
                  {
                    text: "Cancel",
                    onPress: () => {
                      setMapVisible(false);
                      setCurrentStep('none');
                      setModalVisible(false);
                    },
                    style: "cancel"
                  }
                ]
              );
              setError(`You are too far from ${nearestLoc.title}. Please move closer to check in.`);
            }
          }, 2000);
        },
        err => {
          console.error('Location error:', err);
          setIsLoading(false);
          setMapVisible(false);
          setError(`Location error: ${err.message}`);
          Alert.alert("Location Error", err.message);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Location verification failed:', err);
      setIsLoading(false);
      setMapVisible(false);
      setError(`Location verification failed: ${err.message}`);
    }
  };

  // Render face detection overlay
  const renderFaceDetectionOverlay = () => {
    if (!faceDetectionEnabled) return null;
    
    return (
      <View style={styles.faceDetectionOverlay}>
        {faceDetected ? (
          <View style={styles.faceDetectedIndicator}>
            <IconButton icon="face-recognition" size={24} color="#4CAF50" />
            <Text style={styles.faceDetectedText}>Face Detected</Text>
          </View>
        ) : (
          <View style={styles.faceNotDetectedIndicator}>
            <IconButton icon="face-recognition" size={24} color="#FFC107" />
            <Text style={styles.faceNotDetectedText}>Position your face</Text>
          </View>
        )}
        
        {faceBounds && (
          <View
            style={[
              styles.faceBoundsBox,
              {
                left: faceBounds.x,
                top: faceBounds.y,
                width: faceBounds.width,
                height: faceBounds.height,
              }
            ]}
          />
        )}
      </View>
    );
  };

  // Render camera component
  const renderCamera = () => {
    if (!cameraDevice) {
      return (
        <View style={styles.cameraPlaceholder}>
          <IconButton icon="camera-off" size={36} color="#F44336" />
          <Text style={styles.placeholderText}>No camera available</Text>
          <Button 
            mode="contained"
            onPress={async () => {
              const success = await initializeCamera();
              if (success) {
                setCameraInitialized(true);
              }
            }}
            style={{marginTop: 12}}
          >
            Retry Camera
          </Button>
        </View>
      );
    }

    return (
      <>
        <Camera
          ref={cameraRef}
          style={styles.camera}
          device={cameraDevice}
          isActive={currentStep === 'camera' && cameraInitialized}
          photo={true}
          orientation="portrait"
          onInitialized={onCameraReady}
          onError={onCameraError}
          frameProcessor={faceDetectionProcessor}
          frameProcessorFps={5}
        />
        
        {!cameraReady && (
          <View style={styles.cameraLoadingOverlay}>
            <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#FFF" />
            <Text style={styles.cameraLoadingText}>Initializing Camera...</Text>
          </View>
        )}
        
        {renderFaceDetectionOverlay()}
        
        <View style={styles.cameraControlsOverlay}>
          <Button
            mode="contained"
            icon="camera"
            onPress={handleTakePhoto}
            style={styles.captureButton}
            disabled={!cameraReady || !faceDetected || processingPhoto}
            loading={processingPhoto}
          >
            {processingPhoto ? 'Processing...' : 'Verify Face'}
          </Button>
        </View>
      </>
    );
  };

  // Enhance the location verification success display
  const renderLocationSuccess = () => {
    if (currentStep === 'location' && !isLoading && !error && nearestOffice) {
      return (
        <View style={styles.successContainer}>
          <View style={styles.successCircle}>
            <IconButton icon="check" size={36} color="#fff" />
          </View>
          <Text style={styles.successText}>
            Location verified: {nearestOffice.title}
          </Text>
          <Text style={styles.infoText}>
            Distance: {(nearestOffice.distance / 1000).toFixed(2)} km
          </Text>
          {nearestOffice.address && (
            <Text style={styles.addressText}>
              {nearestOffice.address}
            </Text>
          )}
        </View>
      );
    }
    return null;
  };

  // Render map for location verification
  const renderLocationMap = () => {
    if (!mapVisible || !region || !userLocation) return null;
    
    return (
      <View style={styles.mapContainer}>
        <MapView
          ref={mapRef}
          style={styles.map}
          region={region}
          showsUserLocation={true}
          showsMyLocationButton={true}
        >
          {/* User's current position */}
          <Marker
            coordinate={{
              latitude: userLocation.latitude,
              longitude: userLocation.longitude
            }}
            title="Your Location"
            description={`${userLocation.latitude.toFixed(6)}, ${userLocation.longitude.toFixed(6)}`}
            pinColor="blue"
          />

          {/* Office Locations */}
          {officeLocations.map((office, index) => (
            <React.Fragment key={`office-${index}`}>
              <Marker
                coordinate={{
                  latitude: office.latitude,
                  longitude: office.longitude
                }}
                title={office.title}
                description={`${office.latitude.toFixed(6)}, ${office.longitude.toFixed(6)}\nRadius: ${office.radius/1000} km`}
                pinColor={
                  nearestOffice && nearestOffice.title === office.title 
                    ? "red" : "orange"
                }
              />
              <Circle
                center={{
                  latitude: office.latitude,
                  longitude: office.longitude
                }}
                radius={office.radius}
                fillColor="rgba(0, 150, 136, 0.2)"
                strokeColor="rgba(0, 150, 136, 0.5)"
                strokeWidth={2}
              />
            </React.Fragment>
          ))}
        </MapView>
        
        {/* Information overlay on map */}
        {nearestOffice && (
          <View style={styles.mapOverlayInfo}>
            <Text style={styles.mapInfoTitle}>{nearestOffice.title}</Text>
            <Text style={styles.mapInfoCoords}>
              API: {nearestOffice.latitude.toFixed(6)}, {nearestOffice.longitude.toFixed(6)}
            </Text>
            <Text style={styles.mapInfoCoords}>
              You: {userLocation.latitude.toFixed(6)}, {userLocation.longitude.toFixed(6)}
            </Text>
            <Text style={styles.mapInfoDistance}>
              Distance: {(nearestOffice.distance/1000).toFixed(2)} km
            </Text>
            <Text style={[styles.mapInfoStatus, 
              nearestOffice.distance <= nearestOffice.radius 
                ? styles.statusSuccess : styles.statusError]}>
              {nearestOffice.distance <= nearestOffice.radius
                ? "‚úì Within office radius" 
                : "‚úó Outside office radius"}
            </Text>
          </View>
        )}
      </View>
    );
  };

  return (
    <>
      <Card style={styles.card}>
        <Card.Content>
          <View style={styles.statusRow}>
            <View style={[styles.statusBox, checkedIn ? styles.active : styles.inactive]}>
              <Text style={styles.statusText}>Check In {elapsedTime || '00:00:00'}</Text>
            </View>
            <View style={[styles.statusBox, !checkedIn ? styles.active : styles.inactive]}>
              <Text style={styles.statusText}>Check Out 00:00:00</Text>
            </View>
          </View>
          
          <View style={styles.progressContainer}>
            <View style={styles.progressBarBg}>
              <View style={[styles.progressBarFill, { width: `${progressPercentage || 0}%` }]} />
            </View>
            <Text style={styles.progressText}>{progressPercentage || 0}%</Text>
          </View>
          
          <Text style={styles.shiftTime}>Shift: {shiftHours || '00:00'}</Text>
          {shiftCompleted && <Text style={styles.completedText}>Shift Completed</Text>}
          
          <View style={styles.buttonRow}>
            <Button
              mode="contained"
              onPress={handleStartCheckIn}
              disabled={checkedIn}
              style={[styles.button, checkedIn ? styles.disabled : styles.green]}
            >
              Check In
            </Button>
            <Button
              mode="contained"
              onPress={handleStartCheckOut}
              disabled={!checkedIn}
              style={[styles.button, !checkedIn ? styles.disabled : styles.red]}
            >
              Check Out
            </Button>
          </View>
        </Card.Content>
      </Card>

      {/* Camera and location verification modal */}
      <Modal
        visible={modalVisible}
        animationType="slide"
        transparent={true}
        onRequestClose={() => {
          if (!isLoading) setModalVisible(false);
        }}
      >
        <View style={styles.modalOverlay}>
          <View style={styles.modalContent}>
            <Text style={styles.modalTitle}>
              {currentStep === 'location' ? 'Location Verification' :
               currentStep === 'camera' ? 'Face Verification' :
               'Check In'}
            </Text>
            
            {isLoading && (
              <View style={styles.loadingContainer}>
                <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#2196F3" />
                <Text style={styles.loadingText}>
                  {currentStep === 'location' ? 'Verifying your location...' : 
                   currentStep === 'camera' ? 'Processing...' :
                   'Initializing...'}
                </Text>
              </View>
            )}
            
            {/* Map for location verification */}
            {renderLocationMap()}
            
            {/* Show error message when not loading */}
            {error && !isLoading && !mapVisible && (
              <View style={styles.errorContainer}>
                <IconButton icon="alert-circle" size={32} color="#F44336" />
                <Text style={styles.errorText}>{error}</Text>
                <Button 
                  mode="contained" 
                  onPress={() => {
                    setError(null);
                    if (currentStep === 'location') verifyLocationWithMap();
                    else if (currentStep === 'camera') initializeCamera();
                  }}
                  style={styles.retryButton}
                >
                  Retry
                </Button>
              </View>
            )}
            
            {/* Show location success only when not displaying map */}
            {!mapVisible && renderLocationSuccess()}
            
            {currentStep === 'camera' && !isLoading && !error && (
              <View style={styles.cameraContainer}>
                {renderCamera()}
              </View>
            )}
            
            <View style={styles.buttonContainer}>
              <Button
                mode="text"
                onPress={() => {
                  setModalVisible(false);
                  setMapVisible(false);
                }}
                disabled={isLoading}
                style={styles.cancelButton}
              >
                Cancel
              </Button>
            </View>
          </View>
        </View>
      </Modal>
      
      <Snackbar
        visible={snackbarVisible}
        onDismiss={() => setSnackbarVisible(false)}
        duration={2000}
      >
        {snackbarMessage}
      </Snackbar>
    </>
  );
};

export default AttendanceTracker;


import React, { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { View, Text, StyleSheet, Modal, Alert, Platform, ToastAndroid } from 'react-native';
import { Button, ActivityIndicator } from 'react-native-paper';
import Geolocation from '@react-native-community/geolocation';
import axios from 'axios';
import * as geolib from 'geolib';

const API_URL = 'http://192.168.29.2:90/api/';

// Define test coordinates
const TEST_COORDINATES = {
  latitude: 20.304665,
  longitude: 85.863333
};


const GeofencingCamera = ({
  visible,
  onClose,
  geoFenceDetails = [],
}) => {
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const [checkInStatus, setCheckInStatus] = useState('');

  // Toast function that works on both platforms
  const showToast = useCallback((message) => {
    if (Platform.OS === 'android') {
      ToastAndroid.show(message, ToastAndroid.SHORT);
    } else {
      Alert.alert('Notification', message);
    }
  }, []);

  // Test location functionality using actual current location
  const handleTestLocation = async () => {
    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      setError(null);

      // Fetch geo-fence details from the API
      const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}GeoFencing/GetGeoFenceDetails/4`);
      console.log('Geo Fence Details:', response.data);

      const officeLocation = {
        latitude: parseFloat(response.data.lattitude),
        longitude: parseFloat(response.data.longitude),
      };

      // Get user's current location
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        (position) => {
          const userLocation = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };

          console.log('User Location:', userLocation);
          console.log('Office Location:', officeLocation);

          // Calculate distance between user and office in meters
          const distanceInMeters = geolib.getDistance(userLocation, officeLocation);
          console.log('Distance between user and office:', distanceInMeters, 'meters');

          // Check if user is within 50 meters of the office location
          const isWithinRadius = geolib.isPointWithinRadius(userLocation, officeLocation, 50);
          console.log('Is within 50 meter radius:', isWithinRadius);
          
          // Format distance for display
          const formattedDistance = Math.round(distanceInMeters);

          if (isWithinRadius) {
            showToast(`Success: You are ${formattedDistance} meters away from the office location.`);
            Alert.alert(
              "Location Verification Success",
              `You are within the allowed radius.\nDistance: ${formattedDistance} meters from the office location.`,
              [{ text: "OK" }]
            );
          } else {
            showToast(`Failed: You are ${formattedDistance} meters away (exceeds 50 meter limit).`);
            Alert.alert(
              "Location Verification Failed",
              `You are too far from the office location.\nCurrent distance: ${formattedDistance} meters.\nYou need to be within 50 meters to check in.`,
              [{ text: "OK" }]
            );
          }

          setIsLoading(false);
        },
        (err) => {
          setError(`Location error: ${err.message}`);
          setIsLoading(false);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    } catch (err) {
      setError(`API error: ${err.message}`);
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // Test with predefined coordinates
  const handleTestWithFixedCoordinates = async () => {
    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      setError(null);

      // Fetch geo-fence details from the API
      const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}GeoFencing/GetGeoFenceDetails/4`);
      console.log('Geo Fence Details:', response.data);

      const officeLocation = {
        latitude: parseFloat(response.data.lattitude),
        longitude: parseFloat(response.data.longitude),
      };
      
      console.log('Test User Location:', TEST_COORDINATES);
      console.log('Office Location:', officeLocation);

      // Calculate distance between test coordinates and office
      const distanceInMeters = geolib.getDistance(TEST_COORDINATES, officeLocation);
      console.log('Distance between test coordinates and office:', distanceInMeters, 'meters');

      // Check if test coordinates are within 50 meters of the office
      const isWithinRadius = geolib.isPointWithinRadius(TEST_COORDINATES, officeLocation, 50);
      console.log('Is within 50 meter radius:', isWithinRadius);
      
      // Format distance for display
      const formattedDistance = Math.round(distanceInMeters);

      // Show appropriate message based on distance
      if (isWithinRadius) {
        showToast(`Success: Test coordinates are ${formattedDistance} meters from office.`);
        Alert.alert(
          "Test Location Success",
          `The test coordinates are within the allowed radius.\nDistance: ${formattedDistance} meters from the office.`,
          [{ text: "OK" }]
        );
      } else {
        Alert.alert(
          "Test Location Failed",
          `The test coordinates are too far from the office.\nDistance: ${formattedDistance} meters.\nNeeds to be within 50 meters.`,
          [{ text: "OK" }]
        );
      }
      
      setIsLoading(false);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(`API error: ${err.message}`);
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // Handle Check In functionality
  const handleCheckIn = async () => {
    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      setError(null);
      setCheckInStatus('checking');

      // Fetch geo-fence details from the API
      const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}GeoFencing/GetGeoFenceDetails/4`);
      
      const officeLocation = {
        latitude: parseFloat(response.data.lattitude),
        longitude: parseFloat(response.data.longitude),
      };

      // Get user's current location
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        (position) => {
          const userLocation = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };

          // Calculate distance between user and office in meters
          const distanceInMeters = geolib.getDistance(userLocation, officeLocation);
          
          // Check if user is within 50 meters of the office location
          const isWithinRadius = geolib.isPointWithinRadius(userLocation, officeLocation, 50);
          
          // Format distance for display
          const formattedDistance = Math.round(distanceInMeters);

          if (isWithinRadius) {
            setCheckInStatus('success');
            showToast(`Check-in successful! You are ${formattedDistance} meters from the office.`);
            
            // Here you would typically call an API to register the successful check-in
            // For example: axios.post(`${API_URL}/attendance/checkin`, { userId: currentUserId })
            
            setTimeout(() => {
              setCheckInStatus('');
              onClose(); // Close modal after successful check-in
            }, 2000);
          } else {
            setCheckInStatus('failed');
            showToast(`Check-in failed! You are ${formattedDistance} meters away (must be within 50 meters).`);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
              setCheckInStatus('');
            }, 2000);
          }

          setIsLoading(false);
        },
        (err) => {
          setError(`Location error: ${err.message}`);
          setCheckInStatus('');
          setIsLoading(false);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    } catch (err) {
      setError(`API error: ${err.message}`);
      setCheckInStatus('');
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <Modal
      visible={visible}
      animationType="slide"
      transparent={true}
      onRequestClose={() => {
        if (!isLoading) onClose();
      }}
    >
      <View style={styles.modalOverlay}>
        <View style={styles.modalContent}>
          <Text style={styles.modalTitle}>Location Verification</Text>

          {/* Loading indicator */}
          {isLoading && (
            <View style={styles.loadingContainer}>
              <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#2196F3" />
              <Text style={styles.loadingText}>Processing...</Text>
            </View>
          )}

          {/* Error display */}
          {error && !isLoading && (
            <View style={styles.errorContainer}>
              <Text style={styles.errorText}>{error}</Text>
            </View>
          )}

          {/* Check-in Status Display */}
          {checkInStatus === 'success' && !isLoading && (
            <View style={styles.statusContainer}>
              <Text style={styles.successText}>Check-in Successful! ‚úì</Text>
            </View>
          )}
          
          {checkInStatus === 'failed' && !isLoading && (
            <View style={styles.statusContainer}>
              <Text style={styles.errorText}>Check-in Failed! Too far from office.</Text>
            </View>
          )}

          {/* Check In Button */}
          <Button
            mode="contained"
            onPress={handleCheckIn}
            disabled={isLoading}
            style={[styles.testButton, { backgroundColor: '#FF5722' }]}
          >
            Check In
          </Button>

          {/* Test Button */}
          <Button
            mode="contained"
            onPress={handleTestLocation}
            disabled={isLoading}
            style={styles.testButton}
          >
            Test Current Location
          </Button>
          
          {/* Test with Fixed Coordinates Button */}
          <Button
            mode="contained"
            onPress={handleTestWithFixedCoordinates}
            disabled={isLoading}
            style={[styles.testButton, { marginTop: 12, backgroundColor: '#2196F3' }]}
          >
            Test Fixed Coordinates
          </Button>

          {/* Cancel Button */}
          <Button
            mode="text"
            onPress={onClose}
            disabled={isLoading}
            style={styles.cancelButton}
          >
            Cancel
          </Button>
        </View>
      </View>
    </Modal>
  );
};

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  modalOverlay: {
    flex: 1,
    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.4)',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  modalContent: {
    width: '90%',
    backgroundColor: '#fff',
    borderRadius: 12,
    padding: 16,
    alignItems: 'center',
    elevation: 8,
    maxHeight: '80%',
  },
  modalTitle: {
    fontSize: 18,
    fontWeight: 'bold',
    marginBottom: 16,
    color: '#222',
  },
  loadingContainer: {
    width: '100%',
    padding: 20,
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    minHeight: 160,
  },
  loadingText: {
    marginTop: 12,
    fontSize: 16,
    color: '#555',
  },
  errorContainer: {

  cancelButton: {

  },
  statusContainer: {

export default GeofencingCamera;
import React, { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { View, Text, StyleSheet, Alert, Platform, ToastAndroid } from 'react-native';
import { Button, Card, Snackbar, ActivityIndicator } from 'react-native-paper';
import axios from 'axios';
import * as geolib from 'geolib';
import useFetchEmployeeDetails from '../components/FetchEmployeeDetails';

const API_URL = 'http://192.168.29.2:90/api/';

// Test coordinates for checking against office location
const TEST_COORDINATES = {
  latitude: 20.304756,
  longitude: 85.863306
};



// API service for attendance
const attendanceApi = {
  checkIn: async (data) => {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/attendance/check-in`, data);
      return { success: true, data: response.data };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error: error.response?.data?.message || error.message };
    }
  },
  
  checkOut: async (data) => {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/attendance/check-out`, data);
      return { success: true, data: response.data };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error: error.response?.data?.message || error.message };
    }
  }
};

const AttendanceTracker = ({
  checkedIn,
  elapsedTime,
  progressPercentage,
  shiftHours,
  shiftCompleted,
  onCheckIn,
  onCheckOut,
}) => {
  // Employee details from custom hook
  const employeeDetails = useFetchEmployeeDetails();
  
  // State for check-in process
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const [checkInStatus, setCheckInStatus] = useState(''); // 'success', 'failed', or ''
  const [snackbarVisible, setSnackbarVisible] = useState(false);
  const [snackbarMessage, setSnackbarMessage] = useState('');

  // Toast function that works on both platforms
  const showToast = useCallback((message) => {
    setSnackbarMessage(message);
    setSnackbarVisible(true);
    
    if (Platform.OS === 'android') {
      ToastAndroid.show(message, ToastAndroid.SHORT);
    }
  }, []);

  // Handle check-in process with fixed coordinates for testing
  const handleStartCheckIn = async () => {
    try {
      // Reset states
      setError(null);
      setIsLoading(true);
      setCheckInStatus('');
      
      // Fetch geo-fence details from the API
      const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}GeoFencing/GetGeoFenceDetails/4`);
      console.log('Geo Fence Details:', response.data);

      // Extract coordinates and radius from API response
      const officeLocation = {
        latitude: parseFloat(response.data.lattitude),
        longitude: parseFloat(response.data.longitude),
      };
      
      const radiusInMeters = parseInt(response.data.radius) || 50;
      
      console.log('Test User Location:', TEST_COORDINATES);
      console.log('Office Location:', officeLocation);
      console.log('Office Radius (meters):', radiusInMeters);

      // Calculate distance between test coordinates and office
      const distanceInMeters = geolib.getDistance(TEST_COORDINATES, officeLocation);
      console.log('Distance between test coordinates and office:', distanceInMeters, 'meters');

      // Check if test coordinates are within the specified radius of the office
      const isWithinRadius = geolib.isPointWithinRadius(
        TEST_COORDINATES, 
        officeLocation,
        radiusInMeters
      );
      console.log(`Is within ${radiusInMeters} meter radius:`, isWithinRadius);
      
      // Format distance for display
      const formattedDistance = Math.round(distanceInMeters);

      // Simulate a short delay to show loading state
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));

      if (isWithinRadius) {
        setCheckInStatus('success');
        showToast(`Check-in successful! You are ${formattedDistance} meters from the office.`);
        
        // Here you would typically call an API to register the successful check-in
        // For example: axios.post(`${API_URL}/attendance/checkin`, { userId: currentUserId })
        
        // Notify parent component of successful check-in
        if (onCheckIn) onCheckIn();
        
        // Reset status after some time
        setTimeout(() => {
          setCheckInStatus('');
        }, 3000);
      } else {
        setCheckInStatus('failed');
        showToast(`Check-in failed! You are ${formattedDistance} meters away (must be within ${radiusInMeters} meters).`);
        
        Alert.alert(
          "Check-in Failed",
          `You are too far from the office.\nCurrent distance: ${formattedDistance} meters.\nYou need to be within ${radiusInMeters} meters to check in.`,
          [{ text: "OK" }]
        );
        
        // Reset status after some time
        setTimeout(() => {
          setCheckInStatus('');
        }, 3000);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      setError(`Error: ${err.message}`);
      showToast(`Check-in failed: ${err.message}`);
      
      setTimeout(() => {
        setError(null);
      }, 3000);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // Handle check-out process
  const handleStartCheckOut = () => {
    // Directly submit check-out
    submitCheckOut();
  };

  // Check-out submission function
  const submitCheckOut = async () => {
    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      
      // Get current location
      Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        async position => {
          const userPos = {
            latitude: position.coords.latitude,
            longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          };
          
          // Build check-out data
          const checkOutData = {
            employeeId: employeeDetails?.id,
            employeeCode: employeeDetails?.employeeId,
            companyId: employeeDetails?.childCompanyId,
            latitude: userPos.latitude,
            longitude: userPos.longitude,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            checkOutTime: new Date().toISOString(),
          };
          
          // Send check-out data to API
          const result = await attendanceApi.checkOut(checkOutData);
          
          if (result.success) {
            if (onCheckOut) onCheckOut();
            showToast('Check-out successful');
          } else {
            throw new Error(result.error || 'API check-out failed');
          }
        },
        err => {
          showToast(`Location error: ${err.message}`);
        },
        { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 0 }
      );
    } catch (error) {
      showToast('Failed to submit check-out: ' + error.message);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <>
      <Card style={styles.card}>
        <Card.Content>
          <View style={styles.statusRow}>
            <View style={[styles.statusBox, checkedIn ? styles.active : styles.inactive]}>
              <Text style={styles.statusText}>Check In {elapsedTime || '00:00:00'}</Text>
            </View>
            <View style={[styles.statusBox, !checkedIn ? styles.active : styles.inactive]}>
              <Text style={styles.statusText}>Check Out 00:00:00</Text>
            </View>
          </View>
          
          <View style={styles.progressContainer}>
            <View style={styles.progressBarBg}>
              <View style={[styles.progressBarFill, { width: `${progressPercentage || 0}%` }]} />
            </View>
            <Text style={styles.progressText}>{progressPercentage || 0}%</Text>
          </View>
          
          <Text style={styles.shiftTime}>Shift: {shiftHours || '00:00'}</Text>
          {shiftCompleted && <Text style={styles.completedText}>Shift Completed</Text>}
          
          {/* Status Display */}
          {error && (
            <View style={styles.errorContainer}>
              <Text style={styles.errorText}>{error}</Text>
            </View>
          )}
          
          {checkInStatus === 'success' && (
            <View style={styles.statusContainer}>
              <Text style={styles.successText}>Check-in Successful! ‚úì</Text>
            </View>
          )}
          
          {checkInStatus === 'failed' && (
            <View style={styles.statusContainer}>
              <Text style={styles.errorText}>Check-in Failed! Too far from office.</Text>
            </View>
          )}
          
          {/* Button Row */}
          <View style={styles.buttonRow}>
            {isLoading ? (
              <View style={styles.loadingContainer}>
                <ActivityIndicator size="small" color="#4CAF50" />
                <Text style={styles.loadingText}>Processing check-in...</Text>
              </View>
            ) : (
              <>
                <Button
                  mode="contained"
                  onPress={handleStartCheckIn}
                  disabled={checkedIn || isLoading}
                  style={[styles.button, checkedIn ? styles.disabled : styles.green]}
                >
                  Check In
                </Button>
                <Button
                  mode="contained"
                  onPress={handleStartCheckOut}
                  disabled={!checkedIn || isLoading}
                  style={[styles.button, !checkedIn ? styles.disabled : styles.red]}
                >
                  Check Out
                </Button>
              </>
            )}
          </View>
        </Card.Content>
      </Card>
      
      {/* Snackbar for notifications */}
      <Snackbar
        visible={snackbarVisible}
        onDismiss={() => setSnackbarVisible(false)}
        duration={2000}
      >
        {snackbarMessage}
      </Snackbar>
    </>
  );
};

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  card: {
    margin: 8,
    borderRadius: 10,
    elevation: 3,
    backgroundColor: '#fff',
    borderColor: '#ddd',

  },

export default AttendanceTracker;


import React, {useEffect, useState, useRef} from 'react';
import {
  PermissionsAndroid,
  Platform,
  View,
  StyleSheet,
  Text,
  ActivityIndicator,
  Alert,
  TouchableOpacity,
  TextInput,
} from 'react-native';
import Geolocation from '@react-native-community/geolocation';
import MapView, {Marker, PROVIDER_GOOGLE} from 'react-native-maps';
import useFetchEmployeeDetails from '../components/FetchEmployeeDetails';
import {Appbar, FAB, Card, Button, IconButton} from 'react-native-paper';
import AppSafeArea from '../component/AppSafeArea';

const Setting = ({navigation}) => {
  const [location, setLocation] = useState(null);
  const [mapError, setMapError] = useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [tracking, setTracking] = useState(false);
  const [employeeId, setEmployeeId] = useState('');
  const [initialRegion, setInitialRegion] = useState(null);
  const mapRef = useRef(null);
  const watchIdRef = useRef(null);

  // Start tracking right away for better location accuracy
  useEffect(() => {
    startTracking();
    return () => {
      stopTracking();
    };
  }, []);

  const setSpecificLocation = () => {
    getLocation();
  };

  const requestLocationPermission = async () => {
    if (Platform.OS === 'android') {
      const granted = await PermissionsAndroid.request(
        PermissionsAndroid.PERMISSIONS.ACCESS_FINE_LOCATION,
        {
          title: 'Location Permission',
          message: 'App needs access to your location',
          buttonNeutral: 'Ask Me Later',
          buttonNegative: 'Cancel',
          buttonPositive: 'OK',
        },
      );
      return granted === PermissionsAndroid.RESULTS.GRANTED;
    }
    return true;
  };

  const employeeDetails = useFetchEmployeeDetails();

  // Function to post attendance data to the API
  const postAttendanceData = async () => {
    try {
      setLoading(true);
      // Use employee details from the hook or use default values
      const employeeId = employeeDetails?.id || 9;
      const companyId = employeeDetails?.childCompanyId || 1;

      // Make sure location data is available
      if (!location) {
        Alert.alert(
          'Error',
          'Location data is not available. Please try again.',
        );
        setLoading(false);
        return;
      }

      const apiUrl = 'YOUR_API_ENDPOINT_HERE'; // Replace with your actual API endpoint

      // Create payload with detailed location information
      const payload = {
        id: employeeId,
        childCompanyId: companyId,
        // Location data
        latitude: location.latitude,
        longitude: location.longitude,
        // Additional useful fields
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        deviceInfo: Platform.OS + ' ' + Platform.Version,
      };

      console.log('Posting iiiiiiiiiiii data:', payload);

      const response = await fetch(apiUrl, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          // Add any authentication headers if needed
        },
        body: JSON.stringify(payload),
      });

      const responseData = await response.json();

      if (response.ok) {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Attendance marked successfully!');
        console.log('API Response:', responseData);
      } else {
        throw new Error(responseData.message || 'Failed to mark attendance');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error posting attendance data:', error);
      Alert.alert(
        'Error',
        error.message || 'Something went wrong while marking attendance',
      );
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  console.log('Employee==================== Details:', employeeDetails);

  const getLocation = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const hasPermission = await requestLocationPermission();
    if (!hasPermission) {
      setLoading(false);
      Alert.alert(
        'Permission Denied',
        'Location permission is required for this app to work properly.',
      );
      return;
    }

    Geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
      position => {
        const currentLocation = {
          latitude: position.coords.latitude,
          longitude: position.coords.longitude,
          // Add any additional location properties you might need
          accuracy: position.coords.accuracy,
          timestamp: position.timestamp,
        };
        setLocation(currentLocation);

        if (!initialRegion) {
          setInitialRegion({
            ...currentLocation,
            latitudeDelta: 0.005,
            longitudeDelta: 0.005,
          });
        }

        if (mapRef.current) {
          mapRef.current.animateToRegion(
            {
              ...currentLocation,
              latitudeDelta: 0.005,
              longitudeDelta: 0.005,
            },
            1000,
          );
        }

        setLoading(false);
      },
      error => {
        console.error(error);
        Alert.alert(
          'Location Error',
          'Failed to get your location: ' + error.message,
        );
        setLoading(false);
      },
      {
        enableHighAccuracy: true,
        timeout: 15000,
        maximumAge: 0, // Always get fresh location
      },
    );
  };

  const startTracking = async () => {
    setTracking(true);

    // Use the fixed location instead of GPS tracking
    const fixedLocation = {
      latitude: 20.29234264345145,
      longitude: 85.8575183695706,
    };

    setLocation(fixedLocation);

    if (!initialRegion) {
      setInitialRegion({
        ...fixedLocation,
        latitudeDelta: 0.005,
        longitudeDelta: 0.005,
      });
    }
  };

  const stopTracking = () => {
    setTracking(false);
    if (watchIdRef.current !== null) {
      Geolocation.clearWatch(watchIdRef.current);
      watchIdRef.current = null;
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (watchIdRef.current !== null) {
        Geolocation.clearWatch(watchIdRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    getLocation();
  }, []);

  const handleMapError = () => {
    setMapError(true);
  };

  const handleRefresh = () => {
    getLocation();
  };

  const toggleTracking = () => {
    if (tracking) {
      stopTracking();
    } else {
      startTracking();
    }
  };

  const useSpecificLocation = () => {
    setSpecificLocation();
  };

  return (
    <AppSafeArea>
      <Appbar.Header elevated style={styles.header}>
        <Appbar.BackAction onPress={() => navigation.goBack()} />
        <Appbar.Content title="Attendance" titleStyle={styles.headerTitle} />
      </Appbar.Header>
      <View style={styles.container}>
        {location && !mapError ? (
          <>
            <MapView
              ref={mapRef}
              style={styles.map}
              provider={PROVIDER_GOOGLE}
              initialRegion={{
                latitude: 20.29234264345145,
                longitude: 85.8575183695706,
                latitudeDelta: 0.005,
                longitudeDelta: 0.005,
              }}
              showsUserLocation={true}
              followsUserLocation={true}
              onError={handleMapError}>
              <Marker
                coordinate={{
                  latitude: 20.29234264345145,
                  longitude: 85.8575183695706,
                }}
                title="Your Current Location"
                description={`Lat: 20.29234264345145, Lng: 85.8575183695706`}
                pinColor="#2196F3"
              />
            </MapView>

            {/* Refresh FAB */}
            <FAB
              style={styles.refreshFab}
              icon="refresh"
              loading={loading}
              onPress={handleRefresh}
            />

            {/* Bottom Card */}
            <Card style={styles.bottomCard}>
              <Card.Content>
                <View style={styles.cardRow}>
                  <View style={styles.coordinatesBox}>
                    <Text style={styles.cardLabel}>Location Details:</Text>
                    <Text style={styles.coordinatesText}>
                      Latitude: {location.latitude.toFixed(6)}
                    </Text>
                    <Text style={styles.coordinatesText}>
                      Longitude: {location.longitude.toFixed(6)}
                    </Text>
                    <Button
                      mode="contained"
                      style={styles.punchButton}
                      labelStyle={styles.punchButtonLabel}
                      compact={true}
                      onPress={() => {
                        // Share location using the native share dialog
                        const shareMessage = `My current location:\nLatitude: ${location.latitude}\nLongitude: ${location.longitude}`;
                        if (Platform.OS === 'android' || Platform.OS === 'ios') {
                          import('react-native').then(({Share}) => {
                            Share.share({ message: shareMessage });
                          });
                        } else {
                          Alert.alert('Share', shareMessage);
                        }
                      }}
                      loading={loading}>
                      Share
                    </Button>
                    {/* Optionally, keep the attendance button as well */}
                    {/* 
                    <Button
                      mode="contained"
                      style={styles.punchButton}
                      labelStyle={styles.punchButtonLabel}
                      compact={true}
                      onPress={postAttendanceData}
                      loading={loading}>
                      Mark Attendance
                    </Button>
                    */}
                  </View>
                </View>
              </Card.Content>
            </Card>
          </>
        ) : (
          <View style={styles.loader}>
            {mapError ? (
              <View>
                <Text style={styles.errorText}>Map couldn't be loaded</Text>
                <Text>Please check your Google Maps API key</Text>
              </View>
            ) : (
              <>
                <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#0000ff" />
                <Text>Fetching location...</Text>
              </>
            )}
          </View>
        )}
      </View>
    </AppSafeArea>
  );
};

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  container: {
    flex: 1,
    position: 'relative',
  },
  map: {
    flex: 1,
  },
  header: {
    backgroundColor: '#fff',
    elevation: Platform.OS === 'android' ? 4 : 0,
  },
  headerTitle: {
    fontSize: 18,
    fontWeight: 'bold',
    color: '#333',
  },
  loader: {

  },
  errorText: {

  // FAB styles
  refreshFab: {

  // Bottom card styles
  bottomCard: {

  cardRow: {

  },

});

export default Setting;

        headers: {

          // Add any authentication headers if needed
        },
        body: JSON.stringify(payload),
      });

      const responseData = await response.json();

      if (response.ok) {
        Alert.alert('Success', 'Attendance marked successfully!');
        console.log('API Response:', responseData);

        throw new Error(responseData.message || 'Failed to mark attendance');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error posting attendance data:', error);
      Alert.alert(
        'Error',
        error.message || 'Something went wrong while marking attendance',

      setLoading(false);
    }

      position => {
        const currentLocation = {
          latitude: position.coords.latitude,

    setLocation(fixedLocation);

    if (!initialRegion) {
      setInitialRegion({
        ...fixedLocation,
        latitudeDelta: 0.005,
        longitudeDelta: 0.005,

    setTracking(false);
    if (watchIdRef.current !== null) {
      Geolocation.clearWatch(watchIdRef.current);
      watchIdRef.current = null;
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (watchIdRef.current !== null) {
        Geolocation.clearWatch(watchIdRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    getLocation();

  const handleMapError = () => {
    setMapError(true);
  };

  const handleRefresh = () => {
    getLocation();

    if (tracking) {
      stopTracking();
    } else {
      startTracking();
    }
  };

  const useSpecificLocation = () => {
    setSpecificLocation();
  };

  return (
    <AppSafeArea>
      <Appbar.Header elevated style={styles.header}>
        <Appbar.BackAction onPress={() => navigation.goBack()} />
        <Appbar.Content title="Attendance" titleStyle={styles.headerTitle} />

      <View style={styles.container}>

            <MapView
              ref={mapRef}
              style={styles.map}
              provider={PROVIDER_GOOGLE}
              initialRegion={{
                latitude: 20.29234264345145,
                longitude: 85.8575183695706,
                latitudeDelta: 0.005,
                longitudeDelta: 0.005,
              }}
              showsUserLocation={true}
              followsUserLocation={true}
              onError={handleMapError}>
              <Marker
                coordinate={{
                  latitude: 20.29234264345145,
                  longitude: 85.8575183695706,
                }}
                title="Your Current Location"
                description={`Lat: 20.29234264345145, Lng: 85.8575183695706`}
                pinColor="#2196F3"
              />
            </MapView>

            {/* Refresh FAB */}
            <FAB
              style={styles.refreshFab}
              icon="refresh"
              loading={loading}
              onPress={handleRefresh}
            />

            {/* Bottom Card */}
            <Card style={styles.bottomCard}>
              <Card.Content>
                <View style={styles.cardRow}>
                  <View style={styles.coordinatesBox}>
                    <Text style={styles.cardLabel}>Location Details:</Text>
                    <Text style={styles.coordinatesText}>
                      Latitude: {location.latitude.toFixed(6)}
                    </Text>
                    <Text style={styles.coordinatesText}>
                      Longitude: {location.longitude.toFixed(6)}
                    </Text>
                    <Button
                      mode="contained"
                      style={styles.punchButton}
                      labelStyle={styles.punchButtonLabel}
                      compact={true}
                      onPress={() => {
                        // Share location using the native share dialog
                        const shareMessage = `My current location:\nLatitude: ${location.latitude}\nLongitude: ${location.longitude}`;
                        if (Platform.OS === 'android' || Platform.OS === 'ios') {
                          import('react-native').then(({Share}) => {
                            Share.share({ message: shareMessage });
                          });
                        } else {
                          Alert.alert('Share', shareMessage);
                        }
                      }}
                      loading={loading}>
                      Share
                    </Button>
                    {/* Optionally, keep the attendance button as well */}
                    {/* 
                    <Button
                      mode="contained"
                      style={styles.punchButton}
                      labelStyle={styles.punchButtonLabel}
                      compact={true}
                      onPress={postAttendanceData}
                      loading={loading}>
                      Mark Attendance
                    </Button>
                    */}
                  </View>
                </View>
              </Card.Content>
            </Card>
          </>
        ) : (
          <View style={styles.loader}>
            {mapError ? (
              <View>
                <Text style={styles.errorText}>Map couldn't be loaded</Text>
                <Text>Please check your Google Maps API key</Text>
              </View>
            ) : (
              <>
                <ActivityIndicator size="large" color="#0000ff" />
                <Text>Fetching location...</Text>
              </>
            )}
          </View>
        )}
      </View>
    </AppSafeArea>
  );
};

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  container: {
    flex: 1,
    position: 'relative',
  },
  map: {
    flex: 1,
  },
  header: {
